citrā na santi ca  dṛśyante dhātusaṃkṣobhādevaṃ lokaḥ svabhāvataḥ    tṛṇakāṣṭhakaṭhalleṣu yathā māyā virājate  na cāsau vidyate māyā evaṃ dharmāḥ svabhāvataḥ    na grāhako na ca grāhyaṃ na bandhyo na ca bandhanam  māyāmarīcisadṛśaṃ svapnākhyaṃ timiraṃ yathā    yadā paśyati tattvārthī nirvikalpo nirañjanaḥ  tadā yogaṃ samāpanno drakṣyate māṃ na saṃśayaḥ    na hyatra kācidvijñaptirnabhe yadvanmarīcayaḥ  evaṃ dharmān vijānanto na kiṃcitpratijānati    sadasataḥ pratyayeṣu dharmāṇāṃ nāsti saṃbhavaḥ  bhrāntaṃ traidhātuke cittaṃ vicitraṃ khyāyate yataḥ    svapnaṃ ca lokaṃ ca samasvabhāvaṃ rūpāṇi citrāṇi hi tatra cāpi  dṛśyanti bhogaṃ spariśaṃ samānaṃ dehāntagaṃ lokaguruṃ kriyāṃ ca    cittaṃ hi traidhātukayonireta dbhrāntaṃ hi cittamihamutra dṛśyate  na kalpayellokamasatta eṣā metādṛśīṃ lokagatiṃ viditvā    saṃbhavaṃ vibhavaṃ caiva mohātpaśyanti bāliśāḥ  na saṃbhavaṃ na vibhavaṃ prajñāyukto vipaśyati    akaniṣṭhabhavane divye sarvapāpavivarjite  nirvikalpāḥ sadā yuktāścittacaittavivarjitāḥ    balābhijñāvaśiprāptāḥ tatsamādhigatiṃgatāḥ  tatra budhyanti saṃbuddhā nirmitastviha budhyate    nirmāṇakoṭyo hyamitā buddhānāṃ niścaranti ca  sarvatra bālāḥ śṛṇvanti dharmaṃ tebhyaḥ pratiśrutvā     ādimadhyāntanirmuktaṃ bhāvābhāvavivarjitam  vyāpinamacalaṃ śuddhamacitraṃ citrasaṃbhavam    vijñaptigotrasaṃchannamālīnaṃ sarvadehinām  bhrānteśca vidyate māyā na māyā bhrāntikāraṇam    cittasya mohenāpyasti yatkiṃcidapi vidyate  svabhāvadvayanibaddhamālayavijñānanirmitam  lokaṃ vijñaptimātraṃ ca dṛṣṭyaughaṃ dharmapudgalam    vibhāvya lokamevaṃ tu parāvṛtto yadā bhavet  tadā putro bhavenmahyaṃ niṣpannadharmavartakaḥ    uṣṇadravacalakaṭhinā dharmā bālairvikalpitāḥ  asadbhūtasamāropo nāsti lakṣyaṃ na lakṣaṇam    aṣṭadravyakametattu kāyasaṃsthānamindriyam  rūpaṃ kalpanti vai bālā bhrāntāḥ saṃsārapañjare    hetupratyayasāmagryā bālāḥ kalpanti saṃbhavam  ajānānā nayamidaṃ bhramanti tribhavālaye    sarvabhāvāsvabhāvā ca vacanamapi nṛṇām  kalpanāccāpi nirmāṇaṃ nāsti svapnopamaṃ bhavam  parīkṣenna saṃsarennāpi nirvāyāt    cittaṃ vicitraṃ bījākhyaṃ khyāyate cittagocaram  khyātau kalpanti utpattiṃ bālāḥ kalpadvaye ratāḥ    ajñāna tṛṣṇā karmaṃ ca cittacaittā na mārakam  pravartati tato yasmātpāratantryaṃ hi tanmatam    te ca kalpanti yadvastu cittagocaravibhramam  kalpanāyāmaniṣpannaṃ mithyābhrāntivikalpitam    cittaṃ pratyayasaṃbaddhaṃ pravartati śarīriṇām  pratyayebhyo vinirmuktaṃ na paśyāmi vadāmyaham    pratyayebhyo vinirmuktaṃ svalakṣaṇavivarjitam  na tiṣṭhati yadā dehe tena mahyamagocaram    rājā śreṣṭhī yathā putrān vicitrairmṛgasādṛśaiḥ  pralobhya krīḍati gṛhe vane mṛgasamāgamam    tathāhaṃ lakṣaṇaiścitrairdharmāṇāṃ pratibimbakaiḥ  pratyātmavedyāṃ hi sutāṃ bhūtakoṭiṃ vadāmyaham    taraṃgā hyudadheryadvatpavanapratyayoditāḥ  nṛtyamānāḥ pravartante vyucchedaścaḥ na vidyate    ālayaughastathā nityaṃ viṣayapavaneritaḥ  citraistaraṃgavijñānairnṛtyamānaḥ pravartate    grāhyagrāhakabhāvena cittaṃ namati dehinām  dṛśyasya lakṣaṇaṃ nāsti yathā bālairvikalpyate    paramālayavijñānaṃ vijñaptirālayaṃ punaḥ  grāhyagrāhakāpagamāttathatāṃ deśayāmyaham    nāsti skandheṣvātmā na sattvo na ca pudgalaḥ  utpadyate ca vijñānaṃ vijñānaṃ ca nirudhyate    nimnonnataṃ yathā citre dṛśyate na ca vidyate  tathā bhāveṣu bhāvatvaṃ dṛśyate na ca vidyate    gandharvanagaraṃ yadvadyathā ca mṛgatṛṣṇikā  dṛśyaṃ khyāti tathā nityaṃ prajñayā ca na vidyate    pramāṇendriyanirvṛttaṃ na kāryaṃ nāpi kāraṇam  buddhiboddhavyarahitaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitam    skandhān pratītya saṃbuddho na dṛṣṭaḥ kenacitkvacit  yo na dṛṣṭaḥ kvacitkena kutastasya vibhāvanā    pratyayairhetudṛṣṭāntaiḥ pratijñā kāraṇena ca  svapnagandharvacakreṇa marīcyā somabhāskaraiḥ    adṛśyaṃ kulādidṛṣṭāntairutpattiṃ vādayāmyaham  svapnavibhramamāyākhyaṃ śūnyaṃ vai kalpitaṃ jagat    anāśritaśca trailokye adhyātmaṃ ca bahistathā  anutpannaṃ bhavaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣāntyanutpatti jāyate    māyopamasamādhiṃ ca kāyaṃ manomayaṃ punaḥ  abhijñā vaśitā tasya balā cittasya citritā    bhāvā yeṣāṃ hyanutpannāḥ śūnyā vai asvabhāvakāḥ  teṣāmutpadyate bhrāntiḥ pratyayaiśca nirudhyate    cittaṃ hi khyāti cittasya bahirdhā khyāti rūpiṇaḥ  anyanna vidyate dṛśyaṃ yathā bālairvikalpyate    saṃkalā buddhabimbaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ ca vidāraṇam  adhiṣṭhanti jagaccitraṃ prajñaptyā vai suśikṣitāḥ    dehaḥ pratiṣṭhā bhogaśca grāhyavijñaptayastrayaḥ  mana udgrahavijñaptivikalpo grāhakāstrayaḥ    vikalpaśca vikalpyaṃ ca yāvattvakṣaragocaram  tāvattattvaṃ na paśyanti tārkikāstarkavibhramāt    naiḥsvabhāvyaṃ hi bhāvānāṃ yadā budhyanti prajñayā  tadā viśramati yogī ānimittapratiṣṭhitaḥ    masimrakṣitako yadvadgṛhyate kurkuṭobudhaiḥ  sa evāyamajānānairbālairyānatrayaṃ tathā    na hyatra śrāvakāḥ kecinnāsti pratyekayānikāḥ  yaccaitaddṛśyate rūpaṃ śrāvakasya jinasya ca  nirmāṇaṃ deśayantyete bodhisattvāḥ kṛpātmakāḥ    vijñaptimātraṃ tribhavaṃ svabhāvadvayakalpitam  parāvṛttastu tathatā dharmapudgalasaṃcarāt    somabhāskaradīpārcirbhūtāni maṇayastathā  nirvikalpāḥ pravartante tathā buddhasya buddhatā    keśoṇḍukaṃ yathā mithyā gṛhyate taimirairjanaiḥ  tathā bhāvavikalpoyaṃ mithyā bālairvikalpyate    sthitibhaṅgotpattirahitā nityānityavivarjitāḥ  saṃkleśavyavadānākhyā bhāvāḥ keśoṇḍukopamāḥ    puttalikaṃ yathā kaścitkanakābhaṃ paśyate jagat  na hyasti kanakaṃ tatra bhūmiśca kanakāyate    evaṃ hi dūṣitā bālāścittacaittairanādikaiḥ  māyāmarīciprabhavaṃ bhāvaṃ gṛhṇanti tattvataḥ    ekabījamabījaṃ ca samudraikaṃ ca bījakam  sarvabījakamapyetaccittaṃ paśyatha citrikam    ekaṃ bījaṃ yadā śuddhaṃ parāvṛttamabījakam  samaṃ hi nirvikalpatvādudrekājjanmasaṃkaraḥ  bījamāvahate citraṃ sarvabījaṃ taducyate    na hyatrotpadyate kiṃcitpratyayairna nirudhyate  utpadyante nirudhyante pratyayā eva kalpitāḥ    prajñaptimātraṃ tribhavaṃ nāsti vastu svabhāvataḥ  prajñaptivastubhāvena kalpayiṣyanti tārkikāḥ    bhāvasvabhāvajijñāsā na hi bhrāntirnivāryate  bhāvasvabhāvānutpattirevaṃ dṛṣṭvā vimucyate    na māyā nāstisādharmyādbhāvānāṃ kathyatestitā  vitathāśuvidyutsadṛśāstena māyopamāḥ smṛtāḥ    na cotpadyā na cotpannāḥ pratyayopi na kecana  saṃvidyante kvacittena vyavahāraṃ tu kathyate    na bhaṅgotpādasaṃkleśaḥ pratyayānāṃ nivāryate  yattu bālā vikalpenti pratyayaiḥ saṃnivāryate    na svabhāvo na vijñaptirna vastu na ca ālayaḥ  bālairvikalpitā hyete vaśabhūtaiḥ kutārkikaiḥ    cittamātraṃ yadā lokaṃ prapaśyanti jinātmajāḥ  tadā nairvāṇikaṃ kāyaṃ kriyāsaṃskāravarjitam  labhante te balābhijñāvaśitaiḥ saha saṃyutam    sarvarūpāvabhāsaṃ hi yadā cittaṃ pravartate  nātra cittaṃ na rūpāṇi bhrāntaṃ cittamanādikam    tadā yogī hyanābhāsaṃ prajñayā paśyate jagat  nimittaṃ vastuvijñaptirmanovispanditaṃ ca yat  atikramya tu putrā me nirvikalpāścaranti te    gandharvanagaraṃ māyā keśoṇḍuka marīcikā  asatyāḥ satyataḥ khyānti tathā bhāveṣu bhāvanā    anutpannāḥ sarvabhāvā bhrāntimātraṃ hi dṛśyate  bhrāntiṃ kalpenti utpannāṃ bālāṃ kalpadvaye ratāḥ    aupapattyaṅgikaṃ cittaṃ vicitraṃ vāsanāsaṃbhavam  pravartate taraṃgaughaṃ tacchedānna pravartate    vicitrālambanaṃ citraṃ yathā citte pravatate  tathākāśe ca kuḍye ca kasmānnābhipravartate    nimitaṃ kiṃcidālambya yadi cittaṃ pravartate  pratyayairjanitaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate    cittena gṛhyate cittaṃ nāsti kiṃcitsahetukam  cittasya dharmatā śuddhā gagane nāsti vāsanā    svacittābhiniveśena cittaṃ vai saṃpravartate  bahirdhā nāsti vai dṛśyamato vai cittamātrakam    cittamālayavijñānaṃ mano yanmanyanātmakam  gṛhṇāti viṣayān yena vijñānaṃ hi taducyate    cittamavyākṛtaṃ nityaṃ mano hyubhayasaṃcaram  vartamānaṃ hi vijñānaṃ kuśalākuśalaṃ hi tat    dvāraṃ hi paramārthasya vijñaptidvayavarjitam  yānatrayavyavasthānaṃ nirābhāse sthitaṃ kutaḥ    cittamātraṃ nirābhāsaṃ vihārā buddhabhūmiśca  etaddhi bhāṣitaṃ buddhairbhāṣante bhāṣayanti ca    cittaṃ hi bhūmayaḥ sapta nirābhāsā ca aṣṭamī  dve bhūmayo vihāraśca śeṣā bhūmirmamātmikā    pratyātmavedyā śuddhā ca bhūmiścāpi mamātmikā  māheśvaraparasthānamakaniṣṭhe virājate    hutāśanasyaiva yathā niścerustasya raśmayaḥ  citrā manoharāḥ saumyāstribhavaṃ nirmiṇanti ye    nirmāya tribhavaṃ kiṃcitkiṃcidvai pūrvanirmitam  tatra deśanti yānāni eṣā bhūmirmamātmikā    nāsti kālo hyadhigame bhūmīnāṃ kṣatresaṃkrame  cittamātramatikramya nirābhāse sthitaṃ phalam    asattā caiva sattā ca dṛśyate ca vicitratā  bālā grāhaviparyastā viparyāso hi citratā    nirvikalpaṃ yadi jñānaṃ vastvastīti na yujyate  yasmāccittaṃ na rūpāṇi nirvikalpaṃ hi tena tat    indriyāṇi ca māyākhyā viṣayāḥ svapnasaṃnibhāḥ  kartā karma kriyā caiva sarvathāpi na vidyate    dhyānāni cāpramāṇāni ārūpyāśca samādhayaḥ  saṃjñānirodho nikhilaścittamātre na vidyate    srotāpattiphalaṃ caiva sakṛdāgāmiphalaṃ tathā  anāgāmiphalaṃ caiva arhattvaṃ cittavibhramaḥ    śūnyamanityaṃ kṣaṇikaṃ bālāḥ kalpanti saṃskṛtam  nadīdīpādidṛṣṭāntaiḥ kṣaṇikārtho vikalpyate    nirvyāpāraṃ tu kṣaṇikaṃ viviktaṃ kriyavarjitam  anutpattiṃ ca dharmāṇāṃ kṣaṇikārthaṃ vadāmyahyam    saccāsato hyanutpādaḥ sāṃkhyavaiśeṣikaiḥ smṛtaḥ  avyākṛtāni sarvāṇi taireva hi prakāśitam    caturvidhaṃ vyākaraṇamekāṃśaparipṛcchanam  vibhajyasthāpanīyaṃ ca tīrthavādanivāraṇam    sarvaṃ vidyati saṃvṛtyāṃ paramārthe na vidyate  dharmāṇāṃ niḥsvabhāvatvaṃ paramārthepi dṛśyate  upalabdhiniḥsvabhāve saṃvṛtistena ucyate    abhilāpahetuko bhāvaḥ svabhāvo yadi vidyate  abhilāpasaṃbhavo bhāvo nāstīti ca na vidyate    nirvastuko hyabhilāpastatsaṃvṛtyāpi na vidyate  viparyāsasya vastutvāccopalabdhirna vidyate    vidyate cedviparyāso naiḥsvābhāvyaṃ na vidyate  viparyāsasya vastutvādyadyadevopalabhyate  niḥsvabhāvaṃ bhavettaddhi sarvathāpi na vidyate    yadetaddṛśyate citraṃ cittaṃ dauṣṭhulyavāsitam  rūpāvabhāsagrahaṇaṃ bahirdhā cittavibhramam    vikalpenāvikalpena vikalpo hi prahīyate  vikalpenāvikalpena śūnyatātattvadarśanam    māyāhastī yathā citraṃ patrāṇi kanakā yathā  tathā dṛśyaṃ nṛṇāṃ khyāti citte ajñānavāsite    āryo na paśyate bhrāntiṃ nāpi tattvaṃ tadantare  bhrāntireva bhavettattvaṃ yasmāttattvaṃ tadantare    bhrāntiṃ vidhūya sarvāṃ tu nimittaṃ yadi jāyate  saiva cāsya bhavedbhrāntiraśuddhaṃ timiraṃ yathā    keśoṇḍukaṃ taimiriko yathā gṛhṇāti vibhramāt  viṣayeṣu tadvadbālānāṃ grahaṇaṃ saṃpravartate    keśoṇḍukaprakhyamidaṃ marīcyudakavibhramam  tribhavaṃ svapnamāyābhaṃ vibhāvento vimucyate    vikalpaśca vikalpyaśca vikalpasya pravartate  bandho bandhyaśca baddhaśca ṣaḍete mokṣahetavaḥ    na bhūmayo na satyāni na kṣetrā na ca nirmitāḥ  buddhāḥ pratyekabuddhāśca śrāvakāścāpi kalpitāḥ    pudgalaḥ saṃtatiḥ skandhāḥ pratyayā hyaṇavastathā  pradhānamīśvaraḥ kartā cittamātre vikalpyate    cittaṃ hi sarvaṃ sarvatra sarvadeheṣu vartate  vicitraṃ gṛhyatesadbhiścittamātraṃ hyalakṣaṇam    na hyātmā vidyate skandhe skandhāścaiva hi nātmani  na te yathā vikalpyante na ca te vai na santi ca    astitvaṃ sarvabhāvānāṃ yathā bālairvikalpyate  yadi te bhavedyathādṛṣṭāḥ sarve syustattvadarśinaḥ    abhāvātsarvadharmaṇāṃ saṃkleśo nāsti śuddhi ca  na ca te tathā yathādṛṣṭā na ca te vai na santi ca    bhrāntirnimittaṃ saṃkalpaḥ paratantrasya lakṣaṇam  tasminnimitte yannāma tadvikalpitalakṣaṇam    nāmanimittasaṃkalpo yadā tasya na jāyate  pratyayāvastusaṃketaṃ pariniṣpannalakṣaṇam    vaipākikāśca ye buddhā jinā nairmāṇikāśca ye  sattvāśca bodhisattvāśca kṣetrāṇi ca diśe diśe    nisyandadharmanirmāṇā jinā nairmāṇikāśca ye  sarve te hyamitābhasya sukhāvatyā vinirgatāḥ    yacca nairmāṇikairbhāṣṭaṃ yacca bhāṣṭaṃ vipākajaiḥ  sūtrāntavaipulyanayaṃ tasya saṃdhiṃ vijānatha    yadbhāṣitaṃ jinasutairyacca bhāṣanti nāyakāḥ  yaddhi nairmāṇikābhāṣṭaṃ na tu vaipākikairjinaiḥ    anutpannā hyamī dharmā na caivaite na santi ca  gandharvanagarasvapnamāyānirmāṇasādṛśāḥ    cittaṃ pravartate cittaṃ cittameva vimucyate  cittaṃ hi jāyate nānyaccittameva nirudhyate    arthābhāsaṃ nṛṇāṃ cittaṃ cittaṃ vai khyāti kalpitam  nāstyarthaścittamātreyaṃ nirvikalpo vimucyate    anādikālaprapañcadauṣṭhulyaṃ hi samāhitam  vikalpo bhāvitastena mithyābhāsaṃ pravartate    arthābhāse ca vijñāne jñānaṃ tathatāgocaram  parāvṛttaṃ nirābhāsamāryāṇāṃ gocare hyasau    arthapravicayaṃ dhyānaṃ dhyānaṃ bālopacārikam  tathatārambaṇaṃ dhyānaṃ dhyānaṃ tāthāgataṃ śubham    parikalpitaṃ svabhāvena sarvadharmā ajānakāḥ  paratantraṃ samāśritya vikalpo bhramate nṛṇām    paratantraṃ yathā śuddhaṃ vikalpena visaṃyutam  parāvṛttaṃ hi tathatā vihāraḥ kalpavarjitaḥ    mā vikalpaṃ vikalpetha vikalpo nāsti satyataḥ  bhrāntiṃ vikalpayantasya grāhyagrāhakayorna tu  bāhyārthadarśanaṃ kalpaṃ svabhāvaḥ parikalpitaḥ    yena kalpena kalpenti svabhāvaḥ pratyayodbhavaḥ  bāhyārthadarśanaṃ mithyā nāstyarthaṃ cittameva tu    yuktyā vipaśyamānānāṃ grāhagrāhyaṃ nirudhyate  bāhyo na vidyate hyartho yathā bālairvikalpyate    vāsanairlulitaṃ cittamarthābhāsaṃ pravartate  kalpadvayanirodhena jñānaṃ tathatagocaram    utpadyate hyanābhāsamacintyamāryagocaram  nāmanimittasaṃkalpaḥ svabhāvadvayalakṣaṇam  samyagjñānaṃ hi tathatā pariniṣpannalakṣaṇam    mātāpitṛsamāyogādālayamanasaṃyutam  ghṛtakumbhe mūṣikā yadvatsaha śukreṇa vardhate    peśīghanārbudaṃ piṭakamaśubhaṃ karmacitritam  karmavāyumahābhūtaiḥ phalavatsaṃprapadyate    pañcapañcakapañcaiva vraṇāścaiva navaiva tu  nakhadantaromasaṃchannaḥ sphuramāṇaḥ prajāyate    prajātamātraṃ viṣṭhākṛmiṃ suptabuddheva mānavaḥ  cakṣuṣā sphurate rūpaṃ vivṛddhiṃ yāti kalpanāt    tālvoṣṭhapuṭasaṃyogādvikalpenāvadhāryate  vācā pravartate nṝṇāṃ śukasyeva vikalpanā    niścitāstīrthyavādānāṃ mahāyānamaniścitam  sattvāśrayapravṛttoyaṃ kudṛṣṭīnāmanāspadam    pratyātmavedyayānaṃ me tārkikāṇāmagocaram  paścātkāle gate nāthe brūhi koyaṃ dhariṣyati    nirvṛte sugate paścātkālotīto bhaviṣyati  mahāmate nibodha tvaṃ yo netrīṃ dhārayiṣyati    dakṣiṇāpathavedalyāṃ bhikṣuḥ śrīmān mahāyaśāḥ  nāgāhvayaḥ sa nāmnā tu sadasatpakṣadārakaḥ    prakāśya loke madyānaṃ mahāyānamanuttaram  āsādya bhūmiṃ muditāṃ yāsyatesau sukhāvatīm    buddhyā vivecyamānānāṃ svabhāvo nāvadhāryate  yasmāttadanabhilāpyāste niḥsvabhāvāśca deśitāḥ    pratyayotpādite hyarthe nāstyastīti na vidyate  pratyayāntargataṃ bhāvaṃ ye kalpentyasti nāsti ca  dūrībhūtā bhavenmanye śāsanāttīrthadṛṣṭayaḥ    abhidhānaṃ sarvabhāvānāṃ janmāntaraśataiḥ sadā  abhyastamabhyasantaṃ ca parasparavikalpayā    akathyamāne saṃmohaṃ sarvaloka āpadyate  tasmātkriyate nāma saṃmohasya vyudāsārtham    trividhena vikalpena bālairbhāvā vikalpitāḥ  bhrāntirnāmavikalpena pratyayairjanitena ca    aniruddhā hyanutpannāḥ prakṛtyā gaganopamāḥ  abhāvasvabhāvā ye tu te vikalpitalakṣaṇāḥ    pratibhāsabimbamāyābhamarīcyā supinena tu  alātacakragandharvapratiśrutkāsamodbhavāḥ    advayā tathatā śūnyā bhūtakoṣṭiśca dharmatā  nirvikalpaśca deśemi ye te niṣpannalakṣaṇāḥ    vākcittagocaraṃ mithyā satyaṃ prajñā vikalpitā  dvayāntapatitaṃ cittaṃ tasmātprajñā na kalpitā    asti nāsti ca dvāvantau yāvaccittasya gocaraḥ  gocareṇa vidhūtena samyakcittaṃ nirudhyate    viṣayagrahaṇābhāvānnirodhena ca nāsti ca  vidyate tathatāvasthā āryāṇāṃ gocaro yathā    bālānāṃ na tathā khyāti yathā khyāti manīṣiṇām  manīṣiṇāṃ tathā khyāti sarvadharmā alakṣaṇāḥ    hārakūṭaṃ yathā bālaiḥ suvarṇaṃ parikalpyate  asuvarṇaṃ suvarṇābhaṃ tathā dharmāḥ kutārkikaiḥ    abhūtvā yasya cotpādo bhūtvā cāpi vinaśyati  pratyayaiḥ sadasaccāpi na te me śāsane sthitāḥ    anādyanidhanābhāvādbhūtalakṣaṇasaṃsthitāḥ  kāraṇakaravalloke na ca budhyanti tārkikāḥ    atīto vidyate bhāvo vidyate ca anāgataḥ  pratyakṣo vidyate yasmāttasmādbhāvā ajātakāḥ    pariṇāmakālasaṃsthānaṃ bhūtabhāvendriyeṣu ca  antarābhavasaṃgrāhaṃ ye kalpanti na te budhāḥ    na pratītyasamutpannaṃ lokaṃ varṇanti vai jināḥ  kiṃ tu pratyayamevāyaṃ loko gandharvasaṃnibhaḥ    dharmasaṃketa evāyaṃ tasmiṃstadidamucyate  saṃketācca pṛthagbhūto na jāto na nirudhyate    darpaṇe udake netre bhāṇḍeṣu ca maṇīṣu ca  bimbaṃ hi dṛśyate teṣu na ca bimbosti kutracit    bhāvābhāsaṃ tathā cittaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇā yathā nabhe  dṛśyate citrarūpeṇa svapne vandhyauraso yathā    na me yānaṃ mahāyānaṃ na ghoṣo na ca akṣarāḥ  na satyā na vimokṣā vai na nirābhāsagocaram    kiṃ tu yānaṃ mahāyānaṃ samādhivaśavartitā  kāyaṃ manomayaṃ citraṃ vaśitāpuṣpamaṇḍitam    ekatvena pṛthaktvena bhāvo vai pratyaye na tu  janma samāsamevoktaṃ nirodho nāśa eva hi    ajātaśūnyatā caikamekaṃ jāteṣu śūnyatā  ajātaśūnyatā śreṣṭhā naśyate jātaśūnyatā    tathatā śūnyatā koṭī nirvāṇaṃ dharmadhātuvat  kāyo manomayaṃ citraṃ paryāyairdeśitaṃ mayā    sūtravinayābhidharmeṇa viśuddhiṃ kalpayanti ye  granthato na tu arthena na te nairātmyamāśritāḥ    na tīrthikairna buddhaiśca na mayā na ca kenacit  pratyayaiḥ sādhitāstitvaṃ kathaṃ nāstirbhaviṣyati    kena prasādhitāstitvaṃ pratyayairyasya nāstitā  utpādavādadurdṛṣṭyā nāstyastīti vikalpayet    yasya notpadyate kiṃcinna kiṃcittaṃ nirudhyate  tasyāstināsti nopaiti viviktaṃ paśyato jagat    dṛśyate śaśaviṣāṇākhyaṃ vikalpo vidyate nṛṇām  ye tu kalpenti te bhrāntā mṛgatṛṣṇāṃ yathā mṛgāḥ    vikalpābhiniveśena vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  nirhetukaṃ vikalpaṃ hi vikalpopi na yujyate    ajale ca jalagrāho mṛgatṛṣṇā yathā nabhe  dṛśyatertho hi bālānāmāryāṇāṃ na viśeṣataḥ    āryāṇāṃ darśanaṃ śuddhaṃ vimokṣatrayasaṃbhavam  utpādabhaṅganirmuktaṃ nirābhāsapracāriṇam    gāmbhīryodāryavaipulyaṃ jñānaṃ kṣetrān vibhūti ca  deśemi jinaputrāṇāṃ śrāvakāṇāmanityatām    anityaṃ tribhavaṃ śūnyamātmātmīyavivarjitam  śrāvakāṇāṃ ca deśemi tathā sāmānyalakṣaṇam    sarvadharmeṣvasaṃsaktirvivekā hyekacārikā  pratyekajinaputrāṇāṃ phalaṃ deśemyatarkikam    svabhāvakalpitaṃ bāhyaṃ paratantraṃ ca dehinām  apaśyannātmasaṃbhrāntiṃ tataścittaṃ pravartate    daśamī tu bhavetprathamī prathamī cāṣṭamī bhavet  navamī saptamī cāpi saptamī cāṣṭamī bhavet    dvitīyā tu tṛtīyā syāccaturthī pañcamī bhavet  tṛtīyā tu bhavetṣaṣṭhī nirābhāse kramaḥ kutaḥ    nirābhāso hi bhāvānāmabhāvo nāsti yoginām  bhāvābhāvasamatvena āryāṇāṃ jāyate phalam    kathaṃ hyabhāvo bhāvānāṃ kurute samatāṃ katham  yadā cittaṃ na jānāti bāhyamadhyātmikaṃ calam  tadā tu kurute nāśaṃ samatācittadarśanāt    anādimati saṃsāre bhāvagrāhopagūhitam  bālaiḥ kīla yathā kīlaṃ pralobhya vinivartate    taddhetukaṃ tadālambyaṃ manogatisamāśrayam  hetuṃ dadāti cittasya vijñānaṃ ca samāśritam    vaipākikādadhiṣṭhānāṃ nikāyagatisaṃbhavāt  labhyante yena vai svapne abhijñāśca caturvidhāḥ    svapne ca labhyate yacca yacca buddhaprasādataḥ  nikāyagatigotrā ye te vijñānavipākajāḥ    vāsanairbhāvitaṃ cittaṃ bhāvābhāsaṃ pravartate  bālā yadā na budhyante utpādaṃ deśayettadā    yāvadvākyaṃ vikalpeti bhāvaṃ vai lakṣaṇānvitam  tāvadvibudhyate cittamapaśyan hi svavibhramam    utpādo varṇyate kasmātkasmāddṛśyaṃ na varṇyate  adṛśyaṃ dṛśyamānaṃ hi kasya kiṃ varṇyate kutaḥ    svacchaṃ cittaṃ svabhāvena manaḥ kaluṣakārakam  manaśca sahavijñānairvāsanāṃ kṣipate sadā    ālayo muñcate kāyaṃ manaḥ prārthayate gatim  vijñānaṃ viṣayābhāsaṃ bhrāntiṃ dṛṣṭvā pralabhyate    madīyaṃ dṛśyate cittaṃ bāhyamarthaṃ na vidyate  evaṃ vibhāvayedbhrāntiṃ tathatāṃ cāpyanusmaret    dhyāyināṃ viṣayaḥ karma buddhamāhātmyameva ca  etāni trīṇyacintyāni acintyaṃ vijñānagocaram    anāgatamatītaṃ ca nirvāṇaṃ pudgalaṃ vacaḥ  saṃvṛtyā deśayāmyetān paramārthastvanakṣaraḥ    naikāyikāśca tīrthyāśca dṛṣṭimekāṃśamāśritāḥ  cittamātre visaṃmūḍhā bhāvaṃ kalpenti bāhiram    pratyekabodhiṃ buddhatvamarhattvaṃ buddhadarśanam  gūḍhabījaṃ bhavedbodhau svapne vai sidhyate tu yaḥ    kutra keṣāṃ kathaṃ kasmātkimarthaṃ ca vadāhi me  mayācittamatiśāntaṃ sadasatpakṣadeśanām    cittamātre vimūḍhānāṃ māyānāstyastideśanām  utpādabhaṅgasaṃyuktaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitam    vikalpo mano nāma vijñānaiḥ pañcabhiḥ saha  bimbaughajalatulyādau cittabījaṃ pravartate    yadā cittaṃ manaścāpi vijñānaṃ na pravartate  tadā manomayaṃ kāyaṃ labhate buddhabhūmi ca    pratyayā dhātavaḥ skandhā dharmāṇāṃ ca svalakṣaṇam  prajñaptiṃ pudgalaṃ cittaṃ svapnakeśoṇḍukopamāḥ    māyāsvapnopamaṃ lokaṃ dṛṣṭvā tattvaṃ samāśrayet  tattvaṃ hi lakṣaṇairmuktaṃ yuktihetuvivarjitam    pratyātmavedyamāryāṇāṃ vihāraṃ tu smaretsadā  yuktihetuvisaṃmūḍhaṃ lokaṃ tattve niveśayet    sarvaprapañcopaśamādbhrānto nābhipravartate  prajñā yāvadvikalpante bhrāntistāvatpravartate    naiḥsvabhāvyaṃ ca bhāvaṃ ca śūnyā vai nityānityatā  utpādavādināṃ dṛṣṭirna tvanutpādavādinām    ekatvamanyatvobhayāmīśvarācca yadṛcchayā  kālāpradhānādanyebhiḥ pratyayaiḥ kalpyate jagat    saṃsārabījaṃ vijñānaṃ sati dṛśye pravartate  kuḍye sati yathā citraṃ parijñānānnirudhyate    māyāpuruṣavannṝṇāṃ mṛtajanma pravartate  mohāttathaiva bālānāṃ bandhamokṣaṃ pravartate    adhyātmabāhyaṃ dvividhaṃ dharmāśca pratyayāni ca  etadvibhāvayan yogī nirābhāse pratiṣṭhate    na vāsanairbhidyate cittaṃ na cittaṃ vāsanaiḥ saha  abhinnalakṣaṇaṃ cittaṃ vāsanaiḥ pariveṣṭitam    malavadvāsanā yasya manovijñānasaṃbhavā  paṭaśuklopamaṃ cittaṃ vāsanairna virājate    yathā na bhāvo nābhāvo gaganaṃ kathyate mayā  ālayaṃ hi tathā kāye bhāvābhāvavivarjitam    manovijñānavyāvṛttaṃ cittaṃ kāluṣyavarjitam  sarvadharmāvabodhena cittaṃ buddhaṃ vadāmyaham    trisaṃtativyavacchinnaṃ sattāsattāvivarjitam  cātuṣkoṭikayā muktaṃ bhavaṃ māyopamaṃ sadā    dve svabhāvo bhavetsapta bhūmayaścittasaṃbhavāḥ  śeṣā bhaveyurniṣpannā bhūmayo buddhabhūmi ca    rūpī cārūpyadhātuśca kāmadhātuśca nirvṛtiḥ  asmin kalevare sarvaṃ kathitaṃ cittagocaram    upalabhyate yadā yāvadbhrāntistāvatpravartate  bhrāntiḥ svacittasaṃbodhānna pravartate na nivartate    anutpāde kāraṇābhāvo bhāve saṃsārasaṃgrahaḥ  māyādisadṛśaṃ paśyan lakṣaṇaṃ na vikalpayet    triyānamekayānaṃ ca ayānaṃ ca vadāmyaham  bālānāṃ mandabuddhīnāmāryāṇāṃ ca viviktatām    utpattirdvividhā mahyaṃ lakṣaṇādhigamau ca yā  caturvidho nayavidhiḥ siddhāntaṃ yuktideśanā    saṃsthānākṛtiviśeṣairbhrāntiṃ dṛṣṭvā vikalpyate  nāmasaṃsthānavirahātsvabhāvamāryagocaram    vikalpena kalpyate yāvattāvatkalpitalakṣaṇam  vikalpakalpanābhāvātsvabhāvamāryagocaram    nityaṃ ca śāśvataṃ tattvaṃ gotraṃ vastusvabhāvakam  tathatā cittanirmuktaṃ kalpanaiśca vivarjitam    yadyadvastu na śuddhiḥ syātsaṃkleśo nāpi kasyacit  yasmācca śuṃdhyate cittaṃ saṃkleśaścāpi dṛśyate  tasmāttattvaṃ bhavedvastu viśuddhamāryagocaram    pratyayairjanitaṃ lokaṃ vikalpaiśca vivarjitam  māyādisvapnasadṛśaṃ vipaśyanto vimucyate    dauṣṭhulyavāsanāścitrāścittena saha saṃyutāḥ  bahirdhā dṛśyate nṝṇāṃ na hi cittasya dharmatā    cittasya dharmatā śuddhā na cittaṃ bhrāntisaṃbhavam  bhrāntiśca dauṣṭhulyamayī tena cittaṃ na dṛśyate    bhrāntimātraṃ bhavettattvaṃ tattvaṃ nānyatra vidyate  na saṃskāre na cānyatra kiṃ tu saṃskāradarśanāt    lakṣyalakṣaṇanirmuktaṃ yadā paśyati saṃskṛtam  vidhūtaṃ hi bhavettena svacittaṃ paśyato jagat    cittamātraṃ samāruhya bāhyamarthaṃ na kalpayet  tathatālambane sthitvā cittamātramatikramet    cittamātramatikramya nirābhāsamatikramet  nirābhāsasthito yogī mahāyānaṃ sa paśyati    anābhogagatiḥ śāntā praṇidhānairviśodhitā  jñānamanātmakaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ nirābhāse na paśyati    cittasya gocaraṃ paśyetpaśyejjñānasya gocaram  prajñāyā gocaraṃ paśyellakṣaṇe na pramuhyate    cittasya duḥkhasatyaṃ samudayo jñānagocaraḥ  dve satye buddhabhūmiśca prajñā yatra pravartate    phalaprāptiśca nirvāṇaṃ mārgamaṣṭāṅgikaṃ tathā  sarvadharmāvabodhena buddhajñānaṃ viśudhyate    cakṣuśca rūpamāloka ākāśaśca manastathā  ebhirutpadyate nṝṇāṃ vijñānaṃ hyālayodbhavam    grāhyaṃ grāho grahītā ca nāsti nāma hyavastukam  nirhetukaṃ vikalpaṃ ye manyanti hi na te budhāḥ    arthe nāma hyasaṃbhūtamartho nāmni tathaiva ca  hetvahetusamutpannaṃ vikalpaṃ na vikalpayet    sarvabhāvasvabhāvosan vacanaṃ hi tathāpyasat  śūnyatāṃ śūnyatārthaṃ vā bālopaśyan vidhāvati    satyasthitiṃ manyanayā dṛṣṭvā prajñaptideśanā  ekatvaṃ pañcadhāsiddhamidaṃ satyaṃ prahīyate    prapañcamārabhedyaśca astināsti vyatikramet  nāsticchando bhave mithyāsaṃjñā nairātmyadarśanāt    śāśvataṃ hi sakartṛtvaṃ vādamātrapravartitam  satyaṃ paraṃ hyavaktavyaṃ nirodhe dharmadarśanam    ālayaṃ hi samāśritya mano vai saṃpravartate  cittaṃ manaśca saṃśritya vijñānaṃ saṃpravartate    samāropaṃ samāropya tathatā cittadharmatā  etadvibhāvayan yogī cittamātrajñatāṃ labhet    manaśca lakṣaṇaṃ vastu nityānitye na manyate  utpādaṃ cāpyanutpādaṃ yogī yoge na manyate    arthadvayaṃ na kalpenti vijñānaṃ hyālayodbhavam  ekamarthaṃ dvicittena na jānīte tadudbhavam    na vaktā na ca vācyosti na śūnyaṃ cittadarśanāt  adarśanātsvacittasya dṛṣṭijālaṃ pravartate    pratyayāgamanaṃ nāsti indriyāṇi na kecana  na dhātavo na ca skandhā na rāgo na ca saṃskṛtam    karmaṇogniṃ na vai pūrvaṃ na kṛtaṃ na ca saṃskṛtam  na koṭi na ca vai śaktirna mokṣo na ca bandhanam    avyākṛto na bhāvosti dharmādharmaṃ na caiva hi  na kālaṃ na ca nirvāṇaṃ dharmatāpi na vidyate    na ca buddho na satyāni na phalaṃ na ca hetavaḥ  viparyayo na nirvāṇaṃ vibhavo nāsti saṃbhavaḥ    dvādaśāṅgaṃ na caivāsti antānantaṃ na caiva hi  sarvadṛṣṭiprahāṇāya cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham    kleśāḥ karmapathā dehaḥ kartāraśca phalaṃ ca vai  marīcisvapnasaṃkāśā gandharvanagaropamāḥ    cittamātravyavasthānādvayāvṛttaṃ bhāvalakṣaṇam  cittamātrapratiṣṭhānācchāśvatocchedadarśanam    skandhā na santi nirvāṇe na caivātmā na lakṣaṇam  cittamātrāvatāreṇa mokṣagrāhānnivartate    bhūdṛśyahetuko doṣo bahirdhā khyāyate nṛṇām  cittaṃ hyadṛśyasaṃbhūtaṃ tena cittaṃ na dṛśyate    dehabhogapratiṣṭhānā khyāyate vāsanā nṛṇām  cittaṃ na bhāvo nābhāvo vāsane na virājate    malo vai khyāyate śukle na śukle khyāyate malaḥ  ghane hi gaganaṃ yadvattathā cittaṃ na dṛśyate    cittena cīyate karma jñānena ca vicīyate  prajñayā ca nirābhāsaṃ prabhāvaṃ cādhigacchati    cittaṃ viṣayasaṃbaddhaṃ jñānaṃ tarke pravartate  nirābhāse viśeṣe ca jñānaṃ vai saṃpravartate    cittaṃ manaśca vijñānaṃ saṃjñā vai kalpavarjitā  avikalpadharmatāṃ prāptāḥ śrāvakā na jinātmajāḥ    kṣānte kṣānte viśeṣe vai jñānaṃ tāthāgataṃ śubham  saṃjāyate viśeṣārthaṃ samudācāravarjitam    parikalpitasvabhāvosti paratantro na vidyate  kalpitaṃ gṛhyate bhrāntyā paratantraṃ na kalpyate    cittaṃ hyabhūtasaṃbhūtaṃ na cittaṃ dṛśyate kvacit  dehabhogapratiṣṭhānaṃ khyāyate vāsanā nṛṇām    na sarvabhautikaṃ rūpamasti rūpamabhautikam  gandharvasvapnamāyā yā mṛgatṛṣṇā hyabhautikā    prajñā hi trividhā mahyamāryaṃ yena prabhāvitam  cittaṃ hyadṛśyasaṃbhūtaṃ tena cittaṃ na dṛśyate    dehabhogapratiṣṭhānā khyāyate vāsanā nṛṇām  lakṣaṇaṃ kalpate yena yaḥ svabhāvān vṛṇoti ca    yānadvayavisaṃyuktā prajñā hyābhāsavarjitā  saṃbhavābhiniveśena śrāvakāṇāṃ pravartate  cittamātrāvatāreṇa prajñā tāthāgatīmalā    sato hi asataścāpi pratyayairyadi jāyate  ekatvānyatvadṛṣṭiśca avaśyaṃ taiḥ samāśritā    vividhāgatirhi nirvṛttā yathā māyā na sidhyati  nimittaṃ hi tathā citraṃ kalpyamānaṃ na sidhyati    nimittadauṣṭhulyamayaṃ bandhanaṃ cittasaṃbhavam  parikalpitaṃ hyajānānaiḥ paratantraṃ vikalpyate    ya eva kalpito bhāvaḥ paratantraṃ tadeva hi  kalpitaṃ hi vicitrābhaṃ paratantraṃ vikalpyate    saṃvṛtiḥ paramārthaśca tṛtīyaṃ nāsti hetukam  kalpitaṃ saṃvṛtirhyuktā tacchedādāryagocaraḥ    yathā hi yogināṃ vastu citramekaṃ virājate  na hyasti citratā tatra tathā kalpitalakṣaṇam    yathā hi taimiraiścitraṃ kalpyate rūpadarśanam  timiraṃ na rūpaṃ nārūpaṃ paratantraṃ tathā budhaiḥ    hemaṃ syāttu yathā śuddhaṃ jalaṃ kaluṣavarjitam  gaganaṃ hi ghanābhāvāttathā śuddhaṃ vikalpitam    śrāvakastrividho mahyaṃ nirmitaḥ praṇidhānajaḥ  rāgadveṣavisaṃyuktaḥ śrāvako dharmasaṃbhavaḥ    bodhisattvopi trividho buddhānāṃ nāsti lakṣaṇam  citte citte tu sattvānāṃ buddhabimbaṃ vidṛśyate    nāsti vai kalpito bhāvaḥ paratantraṃ ca vidyate  samāropāpavādaṃ ca vikalpaṃ no vinaśyati    kalpitaṃ yadyabhāvaḥ syātparatantrasvabhāvataḥ  vinābhāvena vai bhāvaṃ bhāvaścābhāvasaṃbhavaḥ    parikalpitaṃ samāśritya paratantraṃ pralabhyate  nimittanāmasaṃbandhājjāyate parikalpitam    atyantaṃ cāpyaniṣpannaṃ kalpitena parodbhavam  tadā prajñāyate śuddhaḥ svabhāavaḥ pāramārthikaḥ    parikalpitaṃ daśavidhaṃ paratantraṃ ca ṣaḍvidham  tathatā ca pratyātmagatimato nāsti viśeṣaṇam    pañca dharmā bhavettatvaṃ svabhāvā hi trayastathā  etadvibhāvayan yogī tathatāṃ nātivartate    nakṣatrameghasaṃsthānaṃ somabhāskarasaṃnibham  cittaṃ saṃdṛśyate nṝṇāṃ dṛśyābhaṃ vāsanoditam    bhūtālabdhātmakā hyete na lakṣyaṃ na ca lakṣaṇam  sarve bhūtamayā bhūtā yadi rūpaṃ hi bhautikam    asaṃbhūtā mahābhūtā nāsti bhūteṣu bhautikam  kāraṇaṃ hi mahābhūtāḥ kāryaṃ bhūsalilādayaḥ    dravyaprajñaptirūpaṃ ca māyājātikṛtaṃ tathā  svapnagandharvarūpaṃ ca mṛgatṛṣṇā ca pañcamam    icchantikaṃ pañcavidhaṃ gotrāḥ pañca tathā bhavet  pañca yānānyayānaṃ ca nirvāṇaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ bhavet    skandhabhedāścaturviśadrūpaṃ cāṣṭavidhaṃ bhavet  buddhā bhaveccaturviṃśaddvividhāśca jinaurasāḥ    aṣṭottaraṃ nayaśataṃ śrāvakāśca trayastathā  kṣetramekaṃ hi buddhānāṃ buddhaścaikastathā bhavet    vimuktayastathā tisraścittadhārā caturvidhā  nairātmyaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ mahyaṃ jñeyaṃ cāpi caturvidham    kāraṇaiśca visaṃyuktaṃ dṛṣṭidoṣavivarjitam  pratyātmavedyamacalaṃ mahāyānamanuttaram    utpādaṃ cāpyanutpādamaṣṭadhā navadhā bhavet  ekānupūrvasamayaṃ siddhāntamekameva ca    ārūpyadhātvaṣṭavidhaṃ dhyānabhedaśca ṣaḍvidhaḥ  pratyekajinaputrāṇāṃ niryāṇaṃ saptadhā bhavet    adhvatrayaṃ na caivāsti nityānityaṃ ca nāsti vai  kriyā karma phalaṃ caiva svapnakāryaṃ tathā bhavet    antādyāsaṃbhavā buddhāḥ śrāvakāśca jinaurasāḥ  cittaṃ dṛśyavisaṃyuktaṃ māyādharmopamaṃ sadā    garbhaścakraṃ tathā jātirnaiṣkramyaṃ tuṣitālayam  sarvakṣetragatāścāpi dṛśyante na ca yonijāḥ    saṃkrāntiṃ saṃcaraṃ sattvaṃ deśanā nirvṛtistathā  satyaṃ kṣetrāvabodhiśca pratyayaprerito bhavet    lokā vanaspatirdvīpo nairātmyatīrthasaṃcaram  dhyānaṃ yānālayaprāptiracintyaphalagocaram    candranakṣatragotrāṇi nṛpagotrā surālayam  yakṣagandharvagotrāṇi karmajā tṛṣṇasaṃbhavā    acintyapariṇāmī ca cyutirvāsanasaṃyutā  vyucchinnacyutyabhāvena kleśajālaṃ nirudhyate    dhanadhānyaṃ suvarṇaṃ ca kṣetravastu vikalpyate  gavaiḍakāśca dāsā vai tathā hayagajādayaḥ    talpaviddhe na svaptavyaṃ bhūmiścāpi na lepayet  sauvarṇarājataṃ pātraṃ kāṃsaṃ tāmraṃ na kārayet    kambalā nīlaraktāśca kāṣāyo gomayena ca  kardamaiḥ phalapatraiśca śuklān yogī rajetsadā    śailīkaṃ mṛnmayaṃ lohaṃ śāṅkhaṃ vai sphaṭikamayam  pātrārthaṃ dhārayedyogī paripūrṇaṃ ca māgadham    caturaṅgulaṃ bhavecchastraṃ kubjaṃ vai vastucchedanaḥ  śilpavidyāṃ na śikṣeta yogī yogaparāyaṇaḥ    krayavikrayo na kartavyo yoginā yogivāhinā  ārāmikaiśca kartavyametaddharmaṃ vadāmyaham    guptendriyaṃ tathārthajñaṃ sūtrānte vinaye tathā  gṛhasthairna ca saṃsṛṣṭaṃ yoginaṃ taṃ vadāmyaham    śūnyāgāre śmaśāne vā vṛkṣamūle guhāsu vā  palālebhyavakāśe ca yogī vāsaṃ prakalpayet    trivastraprāvṛto nityaṃ śmaśānādyatrakutracit  vastrārthaṃ saṃvidhātavyaṃ yaśca dadyātsukhāgatam    yugamātrānusārī syātpiṇḍabhakṣaparāyaṇaḥ  kusumebhyo yathā bhramarāstathā piṇḍaṃ samācaret    gaṇe ca gaṇasaṃsṛṣṭe bhikṣuṇīṣu ca yadbhavet  taddhi ājīvasaṃsṛṣṭaṃ na tatkalpati yoginām    rājāno rājaputrāśca amātyāḥ śreṣṭhinastathā  piṇḍārthe nopadeśeta yogī yogaparāyaṇaḥ    mṛtasūtakulānnaṃ ca mitraprītisamanvitam  bhikṣubhikṣuṇisaṃsṛṣṭaṃ na tatkalpati yoginām    vihāre yatra vai dhūmaḥ pacyate vidhivatsadā  uddiśya yatkṛtaṃ cāpi na tatkalpati yoginām    utpādabhaṅganirmuktaṃ sadasatpakṣavarjitam  lakṣyalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ yogī lokaṃ vibhāvayet    samādhibalasaṃyuktamabhijñairvaśitaiśca vai  nacirāttu bhavedyogī yadyutpādaṃ na kalpayet    aṇukālapradhānebhyaḥ kāraṇebhyo na kalpayet  hetupratyayasaṃbhūtaṃ yogī lokaṃ na kalpayet    svakalpakalpitaṃ lokaṃ citraṃ vai vāsanoditam  pratipaśyetsadā yogī māyāsvapnopamaṃ bhavam    apavādasamāropavarjitaṃ darśanaṃ sadā  dehabhogapratiṣṭhābhaṃ tribhavaṃ na vikalpayet    kṛtabhaktapiṇḍo niścitamṛjuṃ saṃsthāpya vai tanum  buddhāṃśca bodhisattvāṃśca namaskṛtya punaḥ punaḥ    vinayātsūtrayuktibhyāṃ tattvaṃ saṃhṛtya yogavit  pañcadharmasvacittaṃ ca nairātmyaṃ ca vibhāvayet    pratyātmadharmatāśuddhā bhūmayo buddhabhūmi ca  etadvibhāvayedyogī mahāpadmebhiṣicyate    vibhrāmya gatayaḥ sarvā bhavādudvegamānasaḥ  yogānārabhate citrāṃ gatvā śivapathīṃ śubhām    somabhāskarasaṃsthānaṃ padmapatrāṃśusaprabham  gaganāgnicitrasadṛśaṃ yogī puñjān prapaśyate    nimittāni ca citrāṇi tīrthyamārgaṃ nayanti te  śrāvakatve nipātyanti pratyekajinagocare    vidhūya sarvāṇyetāni nirābhāso yadā bhavet  tadā buddhakarādityāḥ sarvakṣetrasamāgatāḥ  śiro hi tasya mārjanti nimittaṃ tathatānugāḥ    astyanākārato bhāvaḥ śāśvatocchedavarjitaḥ  sadasatpakṣavigatāḥ kalpayiṣyanti madhyamam    ahetuvāde kalpyante ahetūcchedadarśanam  bāhyabhāvāparijñānānnāśayiṣyanti madhyamam    bhāvagrāhaṃ na mokṣyante mā bhūducchedadarśanam  samāropāpavādena deśayiṣyanti madhyamam    cittamātrāvabodhena bāhyabhāvā vyudāśrayā  vinivṛttirvikalpasya pratipat saiva madhyamā    cittamātraṃ na dṛśyanti dṛśyābhāvānna jāyate  pratipanmadhyamā caiṣā mayā cānyaiśca deśitā    utpādaṃ cāpyanutpādaṃ bhāvābhāvaśca śūnyatā  naiḥsvabhāvyaṃ ca bhāvānāṃ dvayametanna kalpayet    vikalpavṛttyā bhāvo na mokṣaṃ kalpenti bāliśāḥ  na cittavṛttyasaṃbodhāddvayagrāhaḥ prahīyate    svacittadṛśyasaṃbodhāddvayagrāhaḥ prahīyate  prahāṇaṃ hi parijñānaṃ vikalpyasyāvināśakam    cittadṛśyaparijñānādvikalpo na pravartate  apravṛttirvikalpasya tathatā cittavarjitā    tīrthyadoṣavinirmuktā pravṛttiryadi dṛśyate  sā vidvadbhirbhaveddhāhyā nivṛttiścāvināśataḥ    asyāvabodhādbuddhatvaṃ mayā buddhaiśca deśitam  anyathā kalpyamānaṃ hi tīrthyavādaḥ prasajyate    ajāḥ prasūtajanmā vai acyutāśca cyavanti ca  yugapajjalacandrābhā dṛśyante kṣetrakoṭiṣu    ekadhā bahudhā bhūtvā varṣanti ca jvalanti vai  citte cintamayā bhūtvā cittamātraṃ vadanti te    citteṣu cittamātraṃ ca acittā cittasaṃbhavā  vicitrarūpasaṃsthānāścittamātre gatiṃgatāḥ    maunīndraiḥ śrāvakai rūpaiḥ pratyekajinasādṛśaiḥ  anyaiśca vividhai rūpaiścittamātraṃ vadanti te    ārūpyarūpaṃ hyārūpairnārakāṇāṃ ca nārakam  rūpaṃ darśyanti sattvānāṃ cittamātrasya kāraṇam    māyopamaṃ samādhiṃ ca kāyaṃ cāpi manomayam  daśa bhūmīśca vaśitāḥ parāvṛttā labhanti te    svavikalpaviparyāsaiḥ prapañcaspanditaiśca vai  dṛṣṭaśrutamatajñāte bālā badhyanti saṃjñayā    nimittaṃ paratantraṃ hi yannāma tatra kalpitam  parikalpitanimittaṃ pāratantryātpravartate    buddhyā vivecyamānaṃ hi na tantraṃ nāpi kalpitam  niṣpanno nāsti vai bhāvaḥ kathaṃ buddhyā prakalpyate    niṣpanno vidyate bhāvo bhāvābhāvavivarjitaḥ  bhāvābhāvavinirmuktau dvau svabhāvau kathaṃ bhavet    parikalpite svabhāve ca svabhāvau dvau pratiṣṭhitau  kalpitaṃ dṛśyate citraṃ viśuddhamāryagocaram    kalpitaṃ hi vicitrābhaṃ paratantre vikalpyate  anyathā kalpyamānaṃ hi tīrthyavādaṃ samāśrayet    kalpanā kalpanetyuktaṃ darśanāddhetusaṃbhavam  vikalpadvayanirmuktaṃ niṣpannaṃ syāttadeva hi    kṣetraṃ buddhāśca nirmāṇā ekaṃ yānaṃ trayaṃ tathā  na nirvāṇamahaṃ sarve śūnyā utpattivarjitāḥ    ṣaṭtriṃśadbuddhabhedāśca daśa bhedāḥ pṛthakpṛthak  sattvānāṃ cittasaṃtānā ete kṣetrāṇyabhājanam    yathā hi kalpitaṃ bhāvaṃ khyāyate citradarśanam  na hyasti citratā tatra buddhadharmaṃ tathā jagat    dharmabuddho bhavedbuddhaḥ śeṣā vai tasya nirmitāḥ  sattvāḥ svabījasaṃtānaṃ paśyante buddhadarśanaiḥ    bhrāntinimittasaṃbandhādvikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  vikalpā tathatā nānyā na nimittā vikalpanā    svābhāvikaśca saṃbhogo nirmitaṃ pañcanirmitam  ṣaṭtriṃśakaṃ buddhagaṇaṃ buddhaḥ svābhāviko bhavet    nīle raktetha lavaṇe śaṅkhe kṣīre ca śārkare  kaṣāyaiḥ phalapuṣpādyaiḥ kiraṇā yatha bhāskare    na cānye na ca nānanye taraṃgā hyudadhāviva  vijñānāni tathā sapta cittena saha saṃyutā    udadheḥ pariṇāmosau taraṃgāṇāṃ vicitratā  ālayaṃ hi tathā citraṃ vijñānākhyaṃ pravartate    cittaṃ manaśca vijñānaṃ lakṣaṇārthaṃ prakalpyate  abhinnalakṣaṇānyaṣṭau na ca lakṣyaṃ na lakṣaṇam    udadheśca taraṃgāṇāṃ yathā nāsti viśeṣaṇam  vijñānānāṃ tathā citte pariṇāmo na labhyate    cittena cīyate karma manasā ca vicīyate  vijñānena vijānāti dṛśyaṃ kalpeti pañcabhiḥ    nīlaraktaprakāra hi vijñānaṃ khyāyate nṛṇām  taraṃgacittasādharmyaṃ vada kasmānmahāmune    nīlaraktaprakāraṃ hi taraṃgeṣu na vidyate  vṛttiśca varṇyate citte lakṣaṇārthaṃ hi bāliśāḥ    na tasya vidyate vṛttiḥ svacittaṃ grāhyavarjitam  grāhye sati hi vai grāhastaraṃgaiḥ saha sādhyate    dehabhogapratiṣṭhānaṃ vijñānaṃ khyāyate nṛṇām  tenāsya dṛśyate vṛttistaraṃgaiḥ sahasādṛśā    uadadhistaraṃgabhāvena nṛtyamāno vibhāvyate  ālayasya tathā vṛttiḥ kasmādbuddhyā na gṛhyate    bālānāṃ buddhivaikalyādālayaṃ hyudadheryathā  taraṃgavṛttisādharmyā dṛṣṭāntenopanīyate    udeti bhāskaro yadvatsamaṃ hīnottame jane  tathā tvaṃ lokapradyota tattvaṃ deśesi bāliśān    kṛtvā dharmeṣvavasthānaṃ kasmāttattvaṃ na bhāṣase  bhāṣase yadi tattvaṃ vai tattvaṃ citte na vidyate    udadheryathā taraṃgāṇi darpaṇe supine yathā  dṛśyante yugapatkāle tathā cittaṃ svagocare  vaikalyādviṣayāṇāṃ hi kramavṛttyā pravartate    vijñānena vijānāti manasā manyate punaḥ  pañcānāṃ khyāyate dṛśyaṃ kramo nāsti samāhite    citrācāryo yathā kaściccitrāntevāsikopi vā  citrārthe nāmayedraṅgaṃ deśanāpi tathā mama    raṅge na vidyate citraṃ na kuḍye na ca bhājane  sattvānāṃ karṣaṇārthāya raṅgaiścitraṃ vikalpyate    deśanāvyabhicārī ca tattvaṃ hyakṣaravarjitam  kṛtvā dharme vyavasthānaṃ tattvaṃ deśemi yoginām    tattvaṃ pratyātmagatikaṃ kalpyakalpanavarjitam  deśemi jinaputrāṇāṃ bālānāṃ deśanānyathā    vicitrā hi yathā māyā dṛśyate na ca vidyate  deśanā hi tathā citrā dṛśyatevyabhicāriṇī    deśanā hi yadanyasya tadanyasyāpyadeśanā  āture āture yadvadbhiṣagdravyaṃ prayacchati  buddhā hi tadvatsattvānāṃ cittamātraṃ vadanti te    bāhyavāsanabījena vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  tantraṃ hi yena gṛhṇāti yadgṛhṇāti sa kalpitam    bāhyamālambanaṃ gṛhyaṃ cittaṃ cāśritya jāyate  dvidhā pravartate bhrāntistṛtīyaṃ nāsti kāraṇam    yasmācca jāyate bhrāntiryadāśritya ca jāyate  ṣaḍdvādaśāṣṭādaśakaṃ cittameva vadāmyaham    svabījagrāhyasaṃbandhādātmagrāhaḥ prahīyate  cittakalpāvatāreṇa dharmagrāhaḥ prahīyate    yattu ālayavijñānaṃ tadvijñānaṃ pravartate  ādhyātmikaṃ hyāyatanaṃ bhavedbāhyaṃ yadābhayā    nakṣatrakeśagrahaṇaṃ svapnarūpaṃ yathābudhaiḥ  saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtaṃ nityaṃ kalpyate na ca vidyate    gandharvanagaraṃ māyā mṛgatṛṣṇāmbhasāṃ yathā  asanto vā vidṛśyante paratantraṃ tathā bhavet    ātmendriyopacāraṃ hi tricitte deśayāmyaham  cittaṃ manaśca vijñānaṃ svalakṣaṇavisaṃyutā    cittaṃ manaśca vijñānaṃ nairātmyaṃ syāddvayaṃ tathā  pañca dharmāḥ svabhāvā hi buddhānāṃ gocaro hyayam    lakṣaṇena bhavetrīṇī ekaṃ vāsanahetukāḥ  raṅgaṃ hi yathāpyekaṃ kuḍye citraṃ vidṛśyate    nairātmyamadvayaṃ cittaṃ manovijñānameva ca  pañca dharmāḥ svabhāvā hi mama gotre na santi te    cittalakṣaṇanirmuktaṃ vijñānamanavarjitam  dharmasvabhāvavirahaṃ gotraṃ tāthāgataṃ labhet    kāyena vācā manasā na tatra kriyate śubham  gotraṃ tāthāgataṃ śuddhaṃ samudācāravarjitam    abhijñairvaśitaiḥ śuddhaṃ samādhibalamaṇḍitam  kāyaṃ manomayaṃ cittaṃ gotraṃ tāthāgataṃ śubham    pratyātmavedyaṃ hyamalaṃ hetulakṣaṇavarjitam  aṣṭamī buddhabhūmiśca gotraṃ tāthāgataṃ bhavet    dūraṃgamā sādhumatī dharmameghā tathāgatī  etaddhi gotraṃ buddhānāṃ śeṣā yānadvayāvahā    sattvasaṃtānabhedena lakṣaṇārthaṃ ca bāliśām  deśyante bhūmayaḥ sapta buddhaiścittavaśaṃ gatāḥ    vākkāyacittadauṣṭhulyaṃ saptamyāṃ na pravartate  aṣṭamyāṃ hyāśrayastasya svapnaughasamasādṛśaḥ    bhūmyaṣṭamyāṃ ca pañcamyāṃ śilpavidyākalāgamam  kurvanti jinaputrā vai nṛpatvaṃ ca bhavālaye    utpādamatha notpādaṃ śūnyāśūnyaṃ na kalpayet  svabhāvamasvabhāvatvaṃ cittamātre na vidyate    idaṃ tathyamidaṃ tathyamidaṃ mithyā vikalpayet  pratyekaśrāvakāṇāṃ ca deśanā na jinaurasām    saccāsacca sato naiva kṣaṇikaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ na vai  prajñaptidravyasannaiva cittamātre na vidyate    bhāvā vidyanti saṃvṛtyā paramārthe na bhāvakāḥ  niḥsvabhāveṣu yā bhrāntistatsatyaṃ saṃvṛtirbhavet    asatsu sarvadharmeṣu prajñaptiḥ kriyate mayā  abhilāpo vyavahāraśca bālānāṃ tattvavarjitaḥ    abhilāpasaṃbhavo bhāvo vidyate hyarthagocaraḥ  abhilāpasaṃbhavo bhāvo dṛṣṭvā vai nāsti vidyate    kuḍyābhāve yathā citraṃ chāyāyāṃ sthāṇuvarjite  ālayaṃ tu tathā śuddhaṃ taraṃge na virājate    naṭavattiṣṭhate cittaṃ mano vidūṣasādṛśam  vijñānapañcakaiḥ sārdhaṃ dṛśyaṃ kalpati raṅgavat    deśanādharmaniṣyando yacca niṣyandanirmitam  buddhā hyete bhavetpaurāḥ śeṣā nirmāṇavigrahāḥ    dṛśyaṃ na vidyate cittaṃ cittaṃ dṛśyātpramuhyate  dehabhogapratiṣṭhānamālayaṃ khyāyate nṛṇām    cittaṃ manaśca vijñānaṃ svabhāvaṃ dharmapañcakam  nairātmyaṃ dvitayaṃ śuddhaṃ prabhāṣante vināyakāḥ    tārkikāṇāmaviṣayaṃ śrāvakāṇāṃ na caiva hi  yaṃ deśayanti vai nāthā pratyātmagatigocaram    dīrghahrasvādisaṃbaddhamanyonyataḥ pravartate  astitvasādhakā nāsti asti nāstitvasādhakam    aṇuśo vibhajya dravyaṃ na vai rūpaṃ vikalpayet  cittamātravyavasthānaṃ kudṛṣṭyā na prasīdati    mā śūnyatāṃ vikalpetha māśūnyamiti vā punaḥ  nāstyasti kalpanaiveyaṃ kalpyamarthaṃ na vidyate    guṇāṇudravyasaṃghātai rūpaṃ bālairvikalpyate  ekaikamaṇuśo nāsti atopyarthaṃ na vidyate    svacittaṃ dṛśyasaṃsthānaṃ bahirdhā khyāyate nṛṇām  bāhyaṃ na vidyate dṛśyamatopyarthaṃ na vidyate    citraṃ keśoṇḍukaṃ māyāṃ svapna gandharvameva ca  alātaṃ mṛgatṛṣṇā ca asantaṃ khyāyate nṛṇām    nityānityaṃ tathaikatvamubhayaṃ nobhayaṃ tathā  anādidoṣasaṃbaddhā bālāḥ kalpenti mohitāḥ    yānavyavasthā naivāsti yānamekaṃ vadāmyaham  parikarṣaṇārthaṃ bālānāṃ yānabhedaṃ vadāmyaham    vimuktayastathā tisro dharmanairātmyameva ca  samatājñānakleśākhyā vimuktyā te vivarjitāḥ    yathā hi kāṣṭhamudadhau taraṃgairvipravāhyate  tathā ca śrāvako mūḍho lakṣaṇena pravāhyate    niṣṭhāgatirna tattasyā na ca bhūyo nivartate  samādhikāyaṃ saṃprāpya ā kalpānna prabudhyate    vāsanākleśasaṃbaddhā paryutthānairvisaṃyutāḥ  samādhimadamattāste dhātau tiṣṭhantyanāsrave    yathā hi mattaḥ puruṣo madyābhāvādvibudhyate  tathā te buddhadharmākhyaṃ kāyaṃ prāpsyanti māmakam    paṅkamagno yathā hastī itastato na dhāvati  samādhimadamagnā vai tathā tiṣṭhanti śrāvakāḥ    adhiṣṭhānaṃ narendrāṇāṃ praṇīdhānairviśodhitam  abhiṣekasamādhyādyaṃ prathamā daśamī ca vai    ākāśaṃ śaśaśṛṅgaṃ ca vandhyāyāḥ putra eva ca  asantaścābhilapyante tathā bhāveṣu kalpanā    vāsanāhetukaṃ lokaṃ nāsanna sadasatkvacit  ye paśyanti vimucyante dharmanairātmyakovidāḥ    svabhāvakalpitaṃ nāma parabhāvaśca tantrajaḥ  niṣpannaṃ tathatetyuktaṃ sūtre sūtre sadā mayā    vyañjanaṃ padakāyaṃ ca nāma cāpi viśeṣataḥ  bālāḥ sajanti durmedhā yathā paṅke mahāgajāḥ    devayānaṃ brahmayānaṃ śrāvakīyaṃ tathaiva ca  tāthāgataṃ ca pratyekaṃ yānānyetān vadāmyaham    yānānāṃ nāsti vai niṣṭhā yāvaccittaṃ pravartate  citte tu vai parāvṛtte na yānaṃ na ca yāyinaḥ    cittaṃ vikalpo vijñaptirmano vijñānameva ca  ālayaṃ tribhavaśceṣṭā ete cittasya paryayāḥ    āyuruṣmātha vijñānamālayo jīvitendriyam  manaśca manavijñānaṃ vikalpasya viśeṣaṇam    cittena dhāryate kāyo mano manyati vai sadā  vijñānaṃ cittaviṣayaṃ vijñānaiḥ saha chindati    tṛṣṇā hi mātā ityuktā avidyā ca tathā pitā  viṣayāvabodhādvijñānaṃ buddha ityupadiśyate    arhanto hyanuśayāḥ skandhāḥ saṃghaḥ skandhakapañcakaḥ  nirantarāntaracchedātkarma hyānantaraṃ bhavet    nairātmyasya dvayaṃ kleśāstathaivāvaraṇadvayam  acintyapariṇāminyāścyuterlābhāstathāgatāḥ    siddhāntaśca nayaścāpi pratyātmaṃ śāsanaṃ ca vai  ye paśyanti vibhāgajñā na te tarkavaśaṃ gatāḥ    na bhāvo vidyate satyaṃ yathā bālairvikalpyate  abhāvena tu vai mokṣaṃ kathaṃ necchanti tārkikāḥ    utpādabhaṅgasaṃbaddhaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ pratipaśyataḥ  dṛṣṭidvayaṃ prapuṣṇanti na ca jānanti pratyayān    ekameva bhavetsatyaṃ nirvāṇaṃ manavarjitam  kadalīsvapnamāyābhaṃ lokaṃ paśyedvikalpitam    rāgo na vidyate dveṣo mohaścāpi na pudgalaḥ  tṛṣṇāyā hyuditāḥ skandhā vidyante svapnasādṛśāḥ    yasyāṃ ca rātryāṃ dhigamo yasyāṃ ca parinirvṛtaḥ  etasminnantare nāsti mayā kiṃcitprakāśitam    pratyātmadharmasthititāṃ saṃdhāya kathitaṃ mayā  taiśca buddhairmayā caiva na ca kiṃcidviśeṣitam    dravyavadvidyate hyātmā skandhā lakṣaṇavarjitāḥ  skandhā vidyanti bhāvena ātmā teṣu na vidyate    pratipattiṃ vibhāvanto kleśairmānuṣasaṃgamaiḥ  mucyate sarvaduḥkhebhyaḥ svacittaṃ paśyato jagat    kāraṇaiḥ pratyayaiścāpi yeṣāṃ lokaḥ pravartate  cātuṣkoṭikayā yukto na te mannayakovidāḥ    sadasanna jāyate loko nāsanna sadasatkvacit  pratyayaiḥ kāraṇaiścāpi kathaṃ bālairvikalpyate    na sannāsanna sadasadyadā lokaṃ prapaśyati  tadā vyāvartate cittaṃ nairātmyaṃ cādhigacchati    anutpannāḥ sarvabhāvā yasmātpratyayasaṃbhavāḥ  kāryaṃ hi pratyayāḥ sarve na kāryājjāyate bhavaḥ    kāryaṃ na jāyate kāryaṃ dvitvaṃ kārye prasajyate  na ca dvitvaprasaṅgena kāryābhāvopalabhyate    ālambālambavigataṃ yadā paśyati saṃskṛtam  nimittaṃ cittamātraṃ hi cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham    mātrāsvabhāvasaṃsthānaṃ pratyayairbhāvavarjitam  niṣṭhābhāvaparaṃ brahma etāṃ mātrāṃ vadāmyaham    prajñaptisatyato hyātmā dravyaḥ sa hi na vidyate  skandhānāṃ skandhatā tadvatprajñaptyā na tu dravyataḥ    caturvidhā vai samatā lakṣaṇaṃ hetubhājanam  nairātmyasamatā caiva caturthā yogayoginām    vyāvṛttiḥ sarvadṛṣṭīnāṃ kalpyakalpanavarjitā  anupalambho hyajātiśca cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham    na bhāvaṃ nāpi cābhāvaṃ bhāvābhāvavivarjitam  tathatā cittanirmuktaṃ cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham    tathatā śūnyatā koṭī nirvāṇaṃ dharmadhātukam  kāyaṃ manomayaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham    vikalpavāsanābaddhaṃ vicitraṃ cittasaṃbhavam  bahirdhā jāyate nṝṇāṃ cittamātraṃ hi laukikam    dṛśyaṃ na vidyate bāhyaṃ cittacitraṃ vidṛśyate  dehabhogapratiṣṭhābhaṃ cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham    śrāvakāṇāṃ kṣayajñānaṃ buddhānāṃ janmasaṃbhavam  pratyekajinaputrāṇāṃ asaṃkleśātpravartate    bahirdhā nāsti vai rūpaṃ svacittaṃ dṛśyate bahiḥ  anavabodhātsvacittasya bālāḥ kalpenti saṃskṛtam    bāhyamarthamajānānaiḥ svacittacitradarśanam  hetubhirvāryate mūḍhaiścātuṣkoṭikayojitaiḥ    na hetavo na koṭyo vai dṛṣṭāntāvayavāni ca  svacittaṃ hyarthasaṃkrāntaṃ yadi jānanti paṇḍitāḥ    vikalpairna vikalpeta yadvikalpitalakṣaṇam  kalpitaṃ ca samāśritya vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate    anyonyābhinnasaṃbandhādekavāsanahetukāḥ  āgantukatvāttaddvayorna cittaṃ jāyate nṛṇām    vikalpaṃ cittacaittārthī tribhave ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ  yadarthābhāḥ pravartante svabhāvakalpito hi saḥ    ābhāsabījasaṃyogāddvādaśāyatanāni vai  āśrayālambyasaṃyogātprakriyā varṇyate mayā    yathā hi darpaṇe bimbaṃ keśoṇḍustimirasya vā  tathā hi vāsanaiśchannaṃ cittaṃ paśyanti bāliśāḥ    svavikalpakalpite hyarthe vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  artho na vidyate bāhyo yathā tīrthyairvikalpyate    rajjuṃ yathā hyajānānāḥ sarpaṃ gṛhṇanti bāliśāḥ  svacittārthamajānānā hyarthaṃ kalpenti bāhiram    tathā hi rajjuṃ rajjutve ekatvānyatvavarjitam  kiṃ tu svacittadoṣoyaṃ yena rajjurvikalpyate    na hi yo yena bhāvena kalpyamāno na lakṣyate  na tannāstyavagantavyaṃ dharmāṇāmeṣa dharmatā    astitvapūrvakaṃ nāsti asti nāstitvapūrvakam  ato nāsti na gantavyaṃ astitvaṃ na ca kalpayet    kalpitaṃ kalpyamānaṃ hi yadidaṃ na tadātmakam  anātmakaṃ kathaṃ dṛṣṭvā vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate    rūpaṃ rūpātmanā nāsti tathā ghaṭapaṭādayaḥ  avidyamāne dṛśye tu vikalpastena jāyate    vikalpaste yadi bhrāntāvanādimati saṃskṛte  bhāvānāṃ bhāvatā kena bhrāmitā brūhi me mune    bhāvānāṃ bhāvatā nāsti cittamātraṃ ca dṛśyate  apaśyamānaḥ svacittaṃ vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate    kalpitaṃ yadi vai nāsti yathā kalpati bāliśaḥ  anyathā vidyate cāsau na ca buddhyāvagamyate    āryāṇāṃ yadi vā sosti nāsau bālairvikalpitaḥ  āryāṇāmatha mithyāsau āryā bālaiḥ samaṃ gatāḥ    āryāṇāṃ nāsti vai bhrāntiryasmāccittaṃ viśodhitam  aśuddhacittasaṃtānā bālāḥ kalpenti kalpitam    mātā yathā hi putrasya ākāśātphalamānayet  etaddhi putra mā kranda gṛhṇa citramidaṃ phalam    tathāhaṃ sarvasattvānāṃ vicitraiḥ kalpitaiḥ phalaiḥ  pralobhya deśemi nayaṃ sadasatpakṣavarjitam    abhūtvā yasya vai bhāvaḥ pratyayairna ca saṃkulaḥ  ajātapūrvaṃ tajjātamalabdhātmakameva ca    alabdhātmakaṃ hyajātaṃ ca pratyayairna vinā kvacit  utpannamapi te bhāvo pratyayairna vinā kvacit    evaṃ samāsataḥ paśyan nāsanna sadasatkvacit  pratyayairjāyate bhūtamavikalpyaṃ hi paṇḍitaiḥ    ekatvānyatvakathāḥ kutīrthyāḥ kurvanti bāliśāḥ  pratyayairna ca jānanti māyāsvapnopamaṃ jagat    abhidhānaviṣayaṃ yānaṃ mahāyānamanuttaram  arthaṃ sunītaṃ hi mayā na ca budhyanti bāliśāḥ    mātsaryairye praṇītāni śrāvakaistīrthakaistathā  vyabhicaranti te hyarthaṃ yasmāttarkeṇa deśitāḥ    lakṣaṇaṃ bhāva saṃsthānaṃ nāma caiva caturvidham  etadālambanīkṛtya kalpanā saṃpravartate    ekadhā bahudhā ye tu brahmakāyavaśaṃgatāḥ  somabhāskarayorbhāvā ye nāśenti na te sutāḥ    āryadarśanasaṃpannā yathābhūtagatiṃgatāḥ  saṃjñāvivartakuśalā vijñāne ca paraṃgatāḥ    eṣā hi mudrā muktānāṃ putrāṇāṃ mama śāsane  bhāvābhāvavinirmuktā gatyāgativivarjitā    vyāvṛtte rūpavijñāne yadi karma vinaśyati  nityānityaṃ na prāpnoti saṃsāraśca na vidyate    vinirvṛttikāle pradhvastaṃ rūpaṃ deśānnivartate  nāstyastidoṣanirmuktaṃ karma tiṣṭhati ālaye    pradhvaṃsi patitaṃ rūpaṃ vijñānaṃ ca bhavālaye  rūpavijñānasaṃbaddhaṃ na ca karma vinaśyati    atha taiḥ saha saṃbaddhaṃ karma vai dhvasyate nṛṇām  dhvaste tu karmasaṃbandhe na saṃsṛtirna nirvṛtiḥ    atha dhvastamapi taiḥ sārdhaṃ saṃsāre yadi jāyate  rūpaṃ ca tena saṃbaddhamabhinnatvādbhaviṣyati    nābhinnaṃ na ca vai bhinnaṃ cittaṃ rūpaṃ vikalpanāt  pradhvaṃso nāsti bhāvānāṃ sadasatpakṣavarjanāt    kalpitaḥ paratantraśca anyonyābhinnalakṣaṇāt  rūpe hyanityatā yadvadanyonyajanakāśca vai    anyonanyavinirmuktaṃḥ kalpito nāvadhāryate  nāstyasti kathaṃ bhavati rūpe cānityatā yathā    kalpitena sudṛṣṭena paratantro na jāyate  paratantreṇa dṛṣṭena kalpitastathatā bhavet    kalpitaṃ hi vināśete mama netrī vinaśyate  samāropāpavādaṃ ca kurvate mama śāsane    evaṃvidhā yadā yasmin kāle syurdharmadūṣakāḥ  sarve ca te hyasaṃkathyā mama netrīvināśakāḥ    anālapyāśca vidvadbhirbhikṣukāryaṃ ca varjayet  kalpitaṃ yatra nāśenti samāropāpavādinaḥ    keśoṇḍukamāyābhaṃ svapnagandharvasādṛśam  marīcyābhadṛśakalpo yeṣāṃ nāstyastidarśanāt    nāsau śikṣati buddhānāṃ yasteṣāṃ saṃgrahe caret  dvayāntapatitā hyete anyeṣāṃ ca vināśakāḥ    viviktaṃ kalpitaṃ bhāvaṃ ye tu paśyanti yoginaḥ  bhāvābhāvavinirmuktaṃ teṣāṃ vai saṃgrahe caret    ākarā hi yathā loke suvarṇamaṇimuktijāḥ  akarmahetukāścitrā upajīvyāśca bāliśām    tathā hi sattvagotrāṇi citrā vai karmavarjitā  dṛśyābhāvānna karmāsti na ca vai karmajā gatiḥ    bhāvānāṃ bhāvatā nāsti yathā tvāryairvibhāvyate  kiṃ tu vidyanti vai bhāvā yathā bālairvikalpitāḥ    yadi bhāvā va vidyante yathā bālairvikalpitāḥ  asatsu sattvabhāveṣu saṃkleśo nāsti kasyacit    bhāvavaicitryasaṃkleśātsaṃsāraṃ indriyopagaḥ  ajñānatṛṣṇāsaṃbaddhaḥ pravartate śarīriṇām    yeṣāṃ tu bhāvo vai nāsti yathā bālairvikalpitaḥ  teṣāṃ na vidyate vṛttirindriyāṇāṃ na yoginaḥ    yadi bhāvā na vidyante bhāvasaṃsārahetavaḥ  ayaṃ tena bhavenmokṣo bālānāṃ kriyavarjitaḥ    bālāryāṇāṃ viśeṣaste bhāvābhāvātkathaṃ bhavet  āryāṇāṃ nāsti vai bhāvo vimokṣatrayacāriṇām    skandhāśca pudgalā dharmāḥ svasāmānyā alakṣaṇāḥ  pratyayānīndriyāścaiva śrāvakāṇāṃ vadāmyaham    ahetucittamātraṃ tu vibhūti bhūmayastathā  pratyātmatathatāṃ śuddhāṃ deśayāmi jinaurasām    bhaviṣyantyanāgate kāle mama śāsanadūṣakāḥ  kāṣāyavāsovasanāḥ sadasatkāryavādinaḥ    asantaḥ pratyayairbhāvā vidyante hyāryagocaram  kalpito nāsti vai bhāvaḥ kalpayiṣyanti tārkikāḥ    bhaviṣyantyanāgate kāle kaṇabhugbālajātikāḥ  asatkāryavādadurdṛṣṭyā janatāṃ nāśayanti ca    aṇubhyo jagadutpannamaṇavaścāpyahetukāḥ  nava dravyāṇi nityāni kudṛṣṭyā deśayiṣyati    dravyairārabhyate dravyaṃ guṇaiścaiva guṇāstathā  bhāvānāṃ bhāvatāmanyāṃ satīṃ vai nāśayiṣyati    ādimān hi bhavelloko yadyabhūtvā pravartate  pūrvā ca koṭirnaivāsti saṃsārasya vadāmyaham    tribhavaḥ sarvasaṃkhyātaṃ yadyabhūtvā pravartate  śvānoṣṭrakharaśṛṅgāṇāmutpattiḥ syānna saṃśayaḥ    yadyabhūtvā bhaveccakṣū rūpaṃ vijñānameva ca  kaṭamukuṭapaṭādyānāṃ mṛtpiṇḍātsaṃbhavo bhavet    paṭaiśca vai kaṭo nāsti paṭo vai vīraṇaistathā  eka ekatrā saṃbhūtaḥ pratyayaiḥ kiṃ na jāyate    tajjīvaṃ taccharīraṃ ca yaccābhūtvā pravartate  paravādā hyamī sarve mayā ca samudāhṛtāḥ    uccārya pūrvapakṣaṃ ca matisteṣāṃ nivāryate  nivārya tu matisteṣāṃ svapakṣaṃ deśayāmyaham    atorthaṃ tīrthavādānāṃ kṛtamuccāraṇaṃ mayā  mā me śiṣyagaṇo mūḍhaḥ sadasatpakṣamāśrayet    pradhānājjagadutpannaṃ kapilāṅgopi durmatiḥ  śiṣyebhyaḥ saṃprakāśeti guṇānāṃ ca vikāritā    na bhūtaṃ nāpi cābhūtaṃ pratyayairna ca pratyayāḥ  pratyayānāmasadbhāvādabhūtaṃ na pravartate    sadasatpakṣavigato hetupratyayavarjitaḥ  utpādabhaṅgarahitaḥ svapakṣo lakṣyavarjitaḥ    māyāsvapnopamaṃ lokaṃ hetupratyayavarjitam  ahetukaṃ sadā paśyan vikalpo na pravartate    gandharvamṛgatṛṣṇābhaṃ keśoṇḍukanibhaṃ sadā  sadasatpakṣavigataṃ hetupratyayavarjitam  ahetukaṃ bhavaṃ paśyaṃścittadhārā viśudhyate    vastu na vidyate paśyaṃścittamātraṃ na vidyate  avastukaṃ kathaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate    vastumālambanīkṛtya cittaṃ saṃjāyate nṛṇām  ahetukaṃ kathaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate    tathatā cittamātraṃ ca āryavastunayasya tu  vidyante na ca vidyante na te mannayakovidāḥ    grāhyagrāhakabhāvena yadi cittaṃ pravartate  etaddhi laukikaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate    dehabhogapratiṣṭhābhaṃ svapnavajjāyate yadi  dvicittatā prasajyeta na ca cittaṃ dvilakṣaṇam    svadhāraṃ hi yathā khaḍgaṃ svāgraṃ vai aṅguliryathā  na chindate na spṛśate tathā cittaṃ svadarśane    na paraṃ na ca vai tantraṃ kalpitaṃ vastumeva ca  pañca dharmā dvicittaṃ ca nirābhāse na santi vai    utpādakaṃ ca utpādyaṃ dvividhaṃ bhāvalakṣaṇam  utpādakaṃ hi saṃdhāya naiḥsvabhāvyaṃ vadāmyaham    atha vaicitryasaṃsthāne kalpā ca yadi jāyate  ākāśe śaśaśṛṅge ca arthābhāsaṃ bhaviṣyati    arthābhāsaṃ bhaveccittaṃ tadarthaḥ syādakalpitaḥ  na ca vai kalpito hyarthaścittādanyobhilapyate    anādimati saṃsāre artho vai nāsti kutracit  apuṣṭaṃ hi kathaṃ cittamarthābhāsaṃ pravartate    yadyabhāvena puṣṭiḥ syācchaśaśṛṅgepi tadbhavet  na cābhāvena vai puṣṭo vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate    yathāpi dānīṃ naivāsti tathā pūrvepi nāstyasau  anarthe arthasaṃbaddhaṃ kathaṃ cittaṃ pravartate    tathatā śūnyatā koṭirnirvāṇaṃ dharmadhātukam  anutpādaśca dharmāṇāṃ svabhāvaḥ pāramārthikaḥ    nāstyastipatitā bālā hetupratyayakalpanaiḥ  ahetukamanutpannaṃ bhavaṃ vai aprajānataḥ    cittaṃ khyāti na dṛśyosti viśeṣonādihetukaḥ  anādāvapi nāstyartho viśeṣaḥ kena jāyate    yadyabhāvena puṣṭiḥ syāddaridro dhanavān bhavet  arthābhāve kathaṃ cittaṃ jāyate brūhi me mune    ahetukamidaṃ sarvaṃ na cittaṃ na ca gocaraḥ  na ca vai puṣyate cittaṃ tribhavaṃ kriyavarjitam    utpādavinivṛttyarthamanutpādaprasādhanam  ahetuvādaṃ deśemi na ca bālairvibhāvyate  anutpannamidaṃ sarvaṃ na ca bhāvā na santi ca    gandharvasvapnamāyākhyā bhāvā vidyantyahetukāḥ  anutpannān svabhāvāṃśca śūnyāḥ kena vadāsi me    samavāyavinirmukto yadā bhāvo na dṛśyate  tadā śūnyamanutpannamasvabhāvaṃ vadāmyaham    svapnakeśoṇḍukaṃ māyā gandharva mṛgatṛṣṇikā  ahetukā pi dṛśyante tathā lokavicitratā    samavāyastathaivaiko dṛśyābhāvānna vidyate  na tu tīrthyadṛṣṭyā pralayo samavāyo na vidyate    vigṛhyāhetuvādena anutpādaṃ prasādhayet  anutpādaiḥ prasādhyante mama netrī na naśyati    ahetuvādairdeśyante tīrthyānāṃ jāyate bhayam  kathaṃ kena kutaḥ kutra saṃbhavohetuko bhavet    nāhetukamahetutvaṃ yadā paśyanti paṇḍitāḥ  tadā vyāvartate dṛṣṭirbhaṅgotpādānuvādinī    kimabhāvo hyanutpāda utpādotpattilakṣaṇam  atha bhāvasya nāmedaṃ nirarthaṃ vā bravīhi me    na ca bhāvo hyanutpādo na ca pratyayalakṣaṇam  na ca bhāvasya nāmedaṃ na ca nāma nirarthakam    yatra śrāvakabuddhānāṃ tīrthyānāṃ ca agocaraḥ  saptabhūmigatānāṃ ca tadanutpādalakṣaṇam    hetupratyayavyāvṛttiṃ kāraṇasya niṣedhanam  cittamātravyavasthānamanutpādaṃ vadāmyaham    ahetuvṛttiṃ bhāvānāṃ kalpyakalpavivarjitām  sadasatpakṣanirmuktamanutpādaṃ vadāmyaham    cittadṛśyavinirmuktaṃ svabhāvadvayavarjitam  āśrayasya parāvṛttimanutpādaṃ vadāmyaham    na bāhyabhāvaṃ bhāvānāṃ na ca cittaparigraham  sarvadṛṣṭiprahāṇaṃ yattadanutpādalakṣaṇam    evaṃ śūnyāsvabhāvādyān sarvadharmān vibhāvayet  na jātu śūnyayā śūnyā kiṃ tvanutpādaśūnyayā    kalāpaḥ pratyayānāṃ hi pravartate nivartate  kalapācca pṛthagbhūtaṃ na jātaṃ na nirudhyate    bhāvo na vidyate hyanyaḥ kalāpācca pṛthak kvacit  ekatvena pṛthaktvena yathā tīrthyairvikalpyate    sadasanna jāyate bhāvo nāsanna sadasatkvacit  anyatra hi kalāpoyaṃ pravartate nivartate    saṃketamātramevedamanyonyāpekṣasaṃkalāt  janyamarthaṃ na caivāsti pṛthakpratyayasaṃkalāt    janyābhāvo hyanutpādaḥ tīrthyadoṣavivarjitaḥ  deśemi saṃkalāmātraṃ na ca bālairvibhāvyate    yasya janyo hi bhāvosti saṃkalāyāḥ pṛthak kvacit  ahetuvādī vijñeyaḥ saṃkalāyā vināśakaḥ    pradīpadravyajātīnāṃ vyañjakā saṃkalā bhavet  yasya bhāvo bhavetkaścitsaṃkalāyāḥ pṛthak kvacit    asvabhāvo hyanutpannaḥ prakṛtyā gaganopamaḥ  saṃkalāyāḥ pṛthagbhūto yo dharmaḥ kalpitobudhaiḥ    ayamanyamanutpādamāryāṇāṃ prāptidharmatā  yaśca tasya anutpādaṃ tadanutpādakṣāntiḥ syāt    yadā sarvamimaṃ lokaṃ saṃkalāmeva paśyati  saṃkalāmātramevedaṃ tadā cittaṃ samādhyate    ajñānatṛṣṇākarmādi saṃkalādhyātmikā bhavet  khajamṛddaṇḍacakrādi bījabhūtādi bāhiram    parato yasya vai bhāvaḥ pratyayairjāyate kvacit  na saṃkalāmātramevedaṃ na te yuktyāgame sthitāḥ    yadi janyo na bhāvosti syādbuddhiḥ kasya pratyayāt  anyonyapratyayā hyete te tena pratyayāḥ smṛtāḥ    uṣṇadravacalakaṭhinā bālairdharmā vikalpitāḥ  kalāpoyaṃ na dharmosti ato vai niḥsvabhāvatā    vaidyā yathāturavaśātkriyābhedaṃ prakurvate  na tu śāstrasya bhedosti doṣabhedastu vidyate    tathāhaṃ sattvasaṃtāne kleśadoṣaiḥ sudūṣitaiḥ  indriyāṇāṃ balaṃ jñātvā nayaṃ deśemi bāliśān    na kleśendriyabhedena śāsanaṃ bhidyate mama  ekameva bhavedyānaṃ mārgamaṣṭāṅgikaṃ śivam    ghaṭapaṭamukuṭaviṣāṇahetukaśaśaviṣāṇānāstitvam  yaddhetusamutpannaṃ sa ca nāsti tevagantavyam    astitvasādhakaṃ nāsti nāsti nāsti na yujyate  astitvaṃ nāstyapekṣyaṃ hi anyonyāpekṣakāraṇam    kiṃcidāśritya punaḥ kiṃcitkhyāyate yasya vai matam  ahetukaṃ yadāśritya kiṃciccāhetukaṃ na tu    atha tadanyamāśritya tadapyanyasya khyāyate  anavasthā prasajyeta kiṃcicca kiṃ ca no bhavet    āśritya parṇakāṣṭhādīn yathā māyā prasajyate  vastu tadvatsamāśritya vaicitryaṃ khyāyate nṛṇām    māyājālaṃ na parṇāni na kāṣṭhaṃ na ca śarkarā  māyaiva dṛśyate bālairmāyākāreṇa cāśrayam    tathā vastu samāśritya yadi kiṃcidvinaśyati  dṛśyakāle dvayaṃ nāsti kathaṃ kiṃcidvikalpyate    vikalpairvikalpitaṃ nāsti vikalpaśca na vidyate  vikalpe hyavidyamāne tu na saṃsṛtirna nirvṛtiḥ    vikalpe hyavidyamāne tu vikalpo na pravartate  apravṛttiṃ kathaṃ cittaṃ cittamātraṃ na yujyate    anekamatibhinnatvācchāsane nāsti sāratā  sārābhāvānna mokṣosti na ca lokavicitratā    bāhyaṃ na vidyate dṛśyaṃ yathā bālairvikalpyate  bimbavatkhyāyate cittaṃ vāsanairbhramaṇīkṛtam    sarvabhāvā hyanutpannā asatsadasaṃbhavāḥ  cittamātramidaṃ sarvaṃ kalpanābhiśca varjitam    bālairbhāvāḥ samākhyātāḥ pratyayairna tu paṇḍitaiḥ  svabhāvacittanirmuktaścittamāryopagaṃ śivam    sāṃkhyā vaiśeṣikā nagnā viprāḥ pāśupatāstathā  asatsaddṛṣṭipatitā viviktārthavivarjitāḥ    niḥsvabhāvā hyanutpannāḥ śūnyā māyopamāmalāḥ  kasyaite deśitā buddhaistvayā ca prativarṇitāḥ    yogināṃ śuddhacittānāṃ dṛṣṭitarkavivarjitāḥ  buddhā deśenti vai yogaṃ mayā ca prativarṇitāḥ    yadi cittamidaṃ sarvaṃ kasmiṃllokaḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ  gamanāgamanaṃ kena dṛśyate bhūtale nṛṇām    śakuniryathā gagane vikalpena samīritaḥ  apratiṣṭhamanālambyaṃ carate bhūtale yathā    tathā hi dehinaḥ sarve vikalpena samīritāḥ  svacitte caṃkramante te gagane śukaniryathā    dehabhogapratiṣṭhābhaṃ brūhi cittaṃ pravartate  ābhā vṛttiḥ kathaṃ kena cittamātraṃ vadāhi me    dehabhogapratiṣṭhāśca ābhā vṛttiśca vāsanaiḥ  saṃjāyate ayuktānāmābhā vṛttirvikalpanaiḥ    viṣayo vikalpito bhāvaścittaṃ viṣayasaṃbhavam  dṛśyacittaparijñānādvikalpo na pravartate    nāma nāmni visaṃyuktaṃ yadā paśyati kalpitam  buddhiboddhavyarahitaṃ saṃskṛtaṃ mucyate tadā    etā buddhirbhavedbodhyaṃ nāma nāmni vibhāvanam  ye tvanyathāvabudhyante na te buddhā na bodhakāḥ    pañca dharmāḥ svabhāvāśca vijñānānyaṣṭa eva ca  dve nairātmye bhavetkṛtsno mahāyānaparigrahaḥ    yadā buddhiśca boddhavyaṃ viviktaṃ paśyate jagat  nāsti nāma vikalpaśca tadā nābhipravartate    kriyākṣaravikalpānāṃ nivṛttiścittadarśanāt  adarśanātsvacittasya vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate    catvārorūpiṇaḥ skandhāḥ saṃkhyā teṣāṃ na vidyate  bhūtairvilakṣaṇai rūpaṃ kathaṃ rūpabahutvatā    lakṣaṇasya parityāgānna bhūtaṃ na ca bhautikam  athānyalakṣaṇai rūpaṃ kasmātskandhairna jāyate    vimuktāyatanaskandhā yadā paśyatyalakṣaṇāḥ  tadā nivartate cittaṃ dharmanairātmyadarśanāt    viṣayendriyabhedena vijñānaṃ jāyateṣṭadhā  lakṣaṇena bhavetrīṇi nirābhāse nivartate    ālayaṃ hi manasyātmā ātmīyaṃ jñānameva ca  pravartate dvayagrāhātparijñānānnivartate    anyānanyavinirmuktaṃ yadā paśyatyasaṃcaram  tadā dvayaṃ na kalpanti ātmā cātmīyameva ca    apravṛttaṃ na puṣṇāti na ca vijñānakāraṇam  kāryakāraṇanirmuktaṃ niruddhaṃ na pravartate    vikalpaṃ cittamātraṃ ca lokaṃ kena vadāhi me  kāraṇaiśca visaṃyuktaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitam    svacittaṃ dṛśyate citraṃ dṛśyākāraṃ vikalpitam  cittadṛśyāparijñānādanyaṃ cittārthasaṃgrahāt    nāstitvadṛṣṭirbhavati yadā buddhyā na paśyati  astitvaṃ hi kathaṃ tasya cittagrāhānna jāyate    vikalpo na bhāvo nābhāvo atostitvaṃ na jāyate  cittadṛśyaparijñānādvikalpo na pravartate    apravṛtti vikalpasya parāvṛtti nirāśrayaḥ  nivārya pakṣāṃścatvāro yadi bhāvā sahetukāḥ    saṃjñāntaraviśeṣoyaṃ kṛtaṃ kena na sādhitaḥ  arthāpattirbhavetteṣāṃ kāraṇādvā pravartate    hetupratyayasaṃyogātkāraṇapratiṣedhataḥ  nityadoṣo nivāryate anityā yadi pratyayāḥ    na saṃbhavo na vibhavo anityatvāddhi bāliśām  na hi naśyamānaṃ kiṃcidvai kāraṇatvena dṛśyate    adṛṣṭaṃ hi kathaṃ kena nānityo jāyate bhavaḥ  saṃgrahaiśca dametsattvān śīlena ca vaśīkaret    prajñayā nāśayeddṛṣṭiṃ vimokṣaiśca vivardhayet  lokāyatamidaṃ sarvaṃ yattīrthyairdeśyate mṛṣā    kāryakāraṇasaddṛṣṭyā svasiddhāntaṃ na vidyate  ahamekaṃ svasiddhāntaṃ kāryakāraṇavarjitaḥ    deśemi śiṣyavargasya lokāyatavivarjitaḥ  cittamātraṃ na dṛśyosti dvidhā cittaṃ vidṛśyate  grāhyagrāhakabhāvena śāśvatocchedavarjitam    yāvatpravartate cittaṃ tāvallokāyataṃ bhavet  apravṛttirvikalpasya svacittaṃ paśyato jagat    āyaṃ kāryābhinirvṛttirvyayaṃ kāryasya darśanam  āyavyayaparijñānādvikalpo na pravartate    nityamanityaṃ kṛtakamakṛtakaṃ parāparam  evamādyāni sarvāṇi tal lokāyatanaṃ bhavet    devāsuramanuṣyāśca tiryakpretayamālayāḥ  gatayaḥ ṣaṭ samākhyātā yatra jāyanti dehinaḥ    hīnautkṛṣṭamadhyena karmaṇā teṣu jāyate  saraṃkṣya kuśalān sarvān viśeṣo mokṣa eva vā    kṣaṇe kṣaṇe tvayā yanmaraṇaṃ upapattiṃ ca  deśyate bhikṣuvargasya abhiprāyaṃ vadāhi me    rūpādrūpāntaraṃ yadvaccittaṃ saṃbhūya bhajyate  tasmāddeśemi śiṣyāṇāṃ kṣaṇajanmaparaṃparām    rūpe rūpe vikalpasya saṃbhavo vibhavastathā  vikalpo hi bhavejjanturvikalponyo na vidyate    kṣaṇe kṣaṇe yanna yuktamidaṃpratyayabhāṣitam  rūpagrāhavinirmuktaṃ na janma na ca bhajyate    pratyayāḥ pratyayotpannā avidyātathatādayaḥ  dharmadvayena vartante advayā tathatā bhavet    pratyayāḥ pratyayotpannā yadi dharmā viśeṣitāḥ  nityādayo bhavetkāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ pratyayo bhavet    nirviśiṣṭaṃ bhavettīrthyaiḥ kāryakāraṇasaṃgrahāt  vādastava ca buddhānāṃ tasmānnāryo mahāmune    śarīre vyāmamātre ca lokaṃ vai lokasamudayam  nirodhagāminī pratipaddeśayāmi jinaurasān    svabhāvatrayagrāheṇa grāhyagrāhavidṛṣṭayaḥ  lokyalokottarān dharmān vikalpenti pṛthagjanāḥ    ataḥ svabhāvagrahaṇaṃ kriyate pūrvapakṣayā  nivārārthaṃ tu dṛṣṭīnāṃ svabhāvaṃ na vikalpayet    chidradoṣānna niyamo na vā cittaṃ pravartate  pravṛttidvayagrāheṇa advayā tathatā bhavet    ajñāna tṛṣṇā karma ca vijñānādyā ayonijāḥ  anavasthākṛtakatvaṃ ca na kṛtvā jāyate bhavaḥ    caturvidhaśca pradhvaṃso bhāvānāṃ kathyatebudhaiḥ  dvidhāvṛttervikalpasya bhāvābhāvo na vidyate  cātuṣkoṭikanirmuktaṃ darśanadvayavarjitam    dvidhāvṛttivikalpaḥ syāddṛṣṭvā nābhipravartate  anutpanneṣu bhāveṣu buddhervyutthānabhāvataḥ    utpanneṣvapi bhāveṣu tatkalpatvānna kalpayet  yuktiṃ vadāhi me nātha dvidhādṛṣṭinivāraṇāt    yathāhamanye ca sadā nāstyasti na visaṃkaret  tīrthavādaasaṃsṛṣṭāḥ śrāvakairjinavarjitāḥ  jinābhisamayacaryāṃ ca jinaputrāvināśataḥ    vimokṣahetvahetuścāpyanutpādaikalakṣaṇaḥ  paryāyairmohayantyetāṃ varjanīyāṃ sadā budhaiḥ    meghābhrakūṭendradhanuḥprakāśā marīcikeśoṇḍukamāyatulyāḥ  bhāvā hi sarve svavikalpasaṃbhavā stīrthyā vikalpenti jagatsvakāraṇaiḥ    anutpādaśca tathatā bhūtakoṭiśca śūnyatā  rūpasya nāmānyetāni abhāvaṃ na vikalpayet    hastaḥ karo yathā loke indraḥ śakraḥ puraṃdaraḥ  tathā hi sarvabhāvānāmabhāvaṃ na vikalpayet    rūpācca śūnyatā nānyā anutpādaṃ tathaiva ca  na kalpayedananyatvāddṛṣṭidoṣaḥ prasajyate    saṃkalpaśca vikalpaśca vastulakṣaṇasaṃgrahāt  dīrghahrasvādimāṇḍalyaṃ parikalpasya saṃgrahāt    saṃkalpo hi bhaveccittaṃ parikalpo manastathā  vikalpo manavijñānaṃ lakṣyalakṣaṇavarjitam    yacca tīrthyairanutpādo yacca mannayadṛṣṭibhiḥ  kalpyate nirviśiṣṭoyaṃ dṛṣṭidoṣaḥ prasajyate    prayojanamanutpādamanutpādārthameva ca  ye vai jānanti yuktijñāstebhibudhyanti mannayam    prayojanaṃ dṛṣṭisaṃkocamanutpādamanālayam  arthadvayaparijñānādanutpādaṃ vadāmyaham    bhāvā vidyantyanutpannā na vā brūhi mahāmune  ahetuvādonutpādo pravṛttistīrthadarśanam    ahetuvādonutpādo vaiṣamyatīrthadarśanam  astināstivinirmuktaṃ cittamātraṃ vadāmyaham    utpādamanutpādaṃ varjayeddṛṣṭihetukam  ahetuvādenutpāde utpāde kāraṇāśrayaḥ    anābhogakriyā nāsti kriyā ceddṛṣṭisaṃkaraḥ  upāyapraṇidhānādyairdṛṣṭimeva vadāhi me  asattvātsarvadharmāṇāṃ maṇḍalaṃ jāyate katham    grāhyagrāhakavisaṃyogānna pravṛttirna nirvṛtiḥ  bhāvādbhāvāntaraṃ dṛṣṭiṃ cittaṃ vai tatsamutthitam    anutpādaśca dharmāṇāṃ kathametadvadāhi me  sattvāścennāvabudhyante ata etatprakāśyate    pūrvottaravirodhaṃ ca sarvaṃ bhāṣya mahāmune  tīrthadoṣavinirmuktaṃ viṣamāhetuvarjitam    apravṛtirnivṛttiśca brūhi me vādināṃvara  astināstivinirmuktaṃ phalahetvavināśakam    bhūmikramānusaṃdhiśca brūhi me dharmalakṣaṇam  dvayāntapatito loko dṛṣṭibhirvyākulīkṛtaḥ    anutpādā utpādādyaiḥ śamaheturna budhyate  maṇḍalaṃ hi na me kiṃcinna ca deśemi dharmatām    dvaye sati hi doṣaḥ syāddvayaṃ buddhairviśodhitam  śūnyāśca kṣaṇikā bhāvā niḥsvabhāvā hyajātikāḥ    kudṛṣṭivādasaṃchannaiḥ kalpyante na tathāgataiḥ  pravṛttiṃ ca nivṛttiṃ ca vikalpasya vadāhi me    yathā yena prakāreṇa jāyate viṣayo mukham  varṇapuṣkalasaṃyogātprapañcaiḥ samudānitam    rūpaṃ dṛṣṭvā bahirdhā vai vikalpaḥ saṃpravartate  tasyaiva hi parijñānādyathābhūtārthadarśanāt  āryagotrānukūlaṃ ca cittaṃ nābhipravartate    pratyākhyāya tu bhūtāni bhāvotpattirna vidyate  bhūtākāraṃ sadā cittamanutpannaṃ vibhāvayet    mā vikalpaṃ vikalpetha nirvikalpā hi paṇḍitāḥ  vikalpaṃ vikalpayaṃstasya dvayameva na nirvṛtiḥ    anutpādapratijñasya māyā ca dṛśyate nayaḥ  māyānirhetusaṃbhūtaṃ hānisiddhāntalakṣaṇam    bimbavaddṛśyate cittamanādimatibhāvitam  arthākāraṃ na cārthosti yathābhūtaṃ vibhāvayet    yathā hi darpaṇe rūpamekatvānyatvavarjitam  dṛśyate na ca tannāsti tathā cotpādalakṣaṇam    gandharvamāyādi yathā hetupratyayalakṣaṇāḥ  tathā hi sarvabhāvānāṃ saṃbhavo na hyasaṃbhavaḥ    vikalpaḥ puruṣākāro dvidhāvṛttyā pravartate  ātmadharmopacāraiśca na ca bālairvibhāvyate    vipulapratyayādhīnaḥ śrāvakopi hyarhaṃstathā  svabalādhīnaṃ jinādhīnaṃ pañcamaṃ śrāvakaṃ nayet    kālāntaraṃ ca pradhvastaṃ paramārthetaretaram  caturvidhamanityatvaṃ bālāḥ kalpentyakovidāḥ    dvayāntapatitā bālā guṇāṇuprakṛtikāraṇaiḥ  mokṣopāyaṃ na jānanti sadasatpakṣasaṃgrahāt    aṅgulyagraṃ yathā bālaiścandraṃ gṛhṇanti durmatiḥ  tathā hyakṣarasaṃsaktāstattvaṃ nāventi māmakam    vilakṣaṇāni bhūtāni rūpabhāvapravartakā  bhūtānāṃ saṃniveśoyaṃ na bhūtairbhautikaṃ kṛtam    agninā dahyate rūpamabdhātuḥ kledanātmakaḥ  vāyunā kīryate rūpaṃ kathaṃ bhūtaiḥ pravartate    rūpaṃ skandhaśca vijñānaṃ dvayametanna pañcakam  paryāyabhedaṃ skandhānāṃ śatadhā deśayāmyaham    cittacaittasya bhedena vartamānaṃ pravartate  vyatibhinnāni rūpāṇi cittaṃ rūpaṃ na bhautikam    nīlādyapekṣaṇaṃ śvetaṃ śvetaṃ nīlaṃ hyapekṣaṇam  kāryakāraṇamutpādya śūnyatā asti nāsti ca    sādhanaṃ sādhakaṃ sādhyaṃ śītoṣṇe lakṣyalakṣaṇam  evamādyāni sarvāṇi tārkikairna prasādhitāḥ    cittaṃ manaśca ṣaḍvānyavijñānānyātmasaṃyutā  ekatvānyatvarahitā ālayoyaṃ pravartate    sāṃkhyā vaiśeṣikā nagnāstārkikā īśvaroditāḥ  sadasatpakṣapatitā viviktārthavivarjitāḥ    saṃsthānākṛtiviśeṣo bhūtānāṃ nāsti bhautikam  tīrthyā vadanti janma bhūtānāṃ bhautikasya ca    anutpannā yato yenye tīrthyāḥ kalpanti kāraṇaiḥ  na ca budhyanti mohena sadasatpakṣamāśritāḥ    cittena saha saṃyuktaṃ visaṃyuktaṃ manādibhiḥ  viśuddhalakṣaṇaṃ sattvaṃ jñānena saha tiṣṭhati    karma yacca bhavedrūpaṃ skandhaviṣayahetukāḥ  sattvāśca nirupādānā ārūpye nāvatiṣṭhati    nairātmyaṃ sattvavāditvaṃ sattvābhāvātprasajyate  nairātmyavādino cchedo vijñānasyāpyasaṃbhavaḥ    catvāraḥ sthitastasya rūpābhāvātkathaṃ bhavet  adhyātmabāhyābhāvādvijñānaṃ na pravartate    antarābhavikāḥ skandhāḥ yathaivecchanti tārkikāḥ  tathārūpyopapannasya bhavorūpo na cāsti kim    aprayatnena mokṣaḥ syātsattvavijñānayorvinā  tīrthyavādo na saṃdeho na ca budhyanti tārkikāḥ    rūpaṃ ca vidyate tatra ārūpye nāsti darśanam  tadabhāvo na siddhānto na yānaṃ na ca yāyinam    indriyaiḥ saha saṃyuktaṃ vijñānaṃ vāsanodbhavam  aṣṭavidhaikadeśaṃ hi kṣaṇe kāle na gṛhṇanti    na pravartati yadā rūpaṃ indriyā na ca indriyaiḥ  ato hi deśeti bhagavān kṣaṇikā indriyādayaḥ    anirdhārya kathaṃ rūpaṃ vijñānaṃ saṃpravartsyate  apravṛttaṃ kathaṃ jñānaṃ saṃsāraṃ janayiṣyati    utpattyanantaraṃ bhaṅgaṃ na deśenti vināyakāḥ  nairantaryaṃ na bhāvānāṃ vikalpaspandite gatau    indriyā indriyārthāśca mūḍhānāṃ na tu paṇḍitāḥ  bālā gṛhṇanti nāmena āryā vai arthakovidāḥ    ṣaṣṭhaṃ hi nirupādānaḥ sopādāno na gṛhyate  anirdhāryaṃ vadantyāryāṃ astidoṣairvivarjitāḥ    śāśvatocchedabhītāśca tārkikā jñānavarjitāḥ  saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtātmānaṃ na viśeṣanti bāliśāḥ    ekatve vidyate dānamanyatve cāpi vidyate  cittena saha caikatvamanyatvaṃ vai manādibhiḥ    nirdhāryate yadā dānaṃ cittaṃ caittābhiśabditam  upādānātkathaṃ tatra ekatvenāvadhāryate    sopādānopalabdhiśca karmajanmakriyādibhiḥ  agnivatsādhayiṣyanti sadṛśāsadṛśairnaryaiḥ    yathā hi agniryugapaddahyate dāhyadāhakau  sopādānastathā hyātmā tārkikaiḥ kiṃ na gṛhyate    utpādādvāpyanutpādāccittaṃ vai bhāsvaraṃ sadā  dṛṣṭāntaṃ kiṃ na kurvanti tārkikā ātmasādhakāḥ    vijñānagahvare mūḍhāstārkikā nayavarjitāḥ  itastataḥ pradhāvanti ātmavādacikīrṣayā    pratyātmagatigamyaśca ātmā vai śuddhilakṣaṇam  garbhastathāgatasyāsau tārkikāṇāmagocaraḥ    upādānaupādātrorvibhāgaskandhayostathā  lakṣaṇaṃ yadi jānāti jñānaṃ saṃjāyate nayam    ālayaṃ garbhasaṃsthānaṃ mataṃ tīrthyānuvarṇitam  ātmanā saha saṃyuktaṃ na ca dharmāḥ prakīrtitāḥ    eteṣāṃ pravibhāgena vimokṣaḥ satyadarśanam  bhāvānāṃ darśyaheyānāṃ kleśānāṃ syādviśodhanam    prakṛtiprabhāsvaraṃ cittaṃ garbhaṃ tāthāgataṃ śubham  upādānaṃ hi sattvasya antānantavivarjitam    kāntiryathā suvarṇasya jātarūpaṃ ca śarkaram  parikarmeṇa paśyanti sattvaṃ skandhālayaistathā    na pudgalo na ca skandhā buddho jñānamanāsravam  sadāśāntiṃ vibhāvitvā gacchāmi śaraṇaṃ hyaham    prakṛtiprabhāsvaraṃ cittamupakleśairmanādibhiḥ  ātmanā saha saṃyuktaṃ deśeti vadatāṃvaraḥ    prakṛtiprabhāsvaraṃ cittaṃ manādyastasya vai paraḥ  tairācitāni karmāṇi yataḥ kliśyanti tāvubhau    āgantukairānādyaiśca kleśairātmā prabhāsvaraḥ  saṃkliśyate upetaśca vastravatpariśudhyate    malābhāvādyathā vastraṃ hemaṃ vā doṣavarjitam  tiṣṭhanti na ca naśyante ātmā doṣaistathā vinā    vīṇāśaṅkhetha bheryāṃ ca mādhuryasvarasaṃpadā  mṛgayeddhyakovidaḥ kaścittathā skandheṣu pudgalam    nidhayo maṇayaścāpi pṛthivyāmudakaṃ tathā  vidyamānā na dṛśyanti tathā skandheṣu pudgalam    cittacaittakalāpāṃśca svaguṇāṃ skandhasaṃyutāṃ  akovidā na gṛhṇanti tathā skandheṣu pudgalam    yathā hi garbho garbhiṇyāṃ vidyate na ca dṛśyate  ātmā hi tadvatskandheṣu ayuktijño na paśyati    auṣadhīnāṃ yathā sāramagniṃ vā indhanairyathā  na paśyanti ayuktijñāstathā skandheṣu pudgalam    anityatāṃ sarvabhāveṣu śūnyatāṃ ca yathābudhāḥ  vidyamānāṃ na paśyanti tathā skandheṣu pudgalam    bhūmayo vaśitābhijñā abhiṣekaṃ ca uttaram  samādhayo viśeṣāśca asatyātmani nāsti vai    vaināśiko yadā gatvā brūyādyadyasti deśyatām  sa vaktavyo bhavedvijñaḥ svavikalpaṃ pradarśaya    nairātmyavādinobhāṣyā bhikṣukarmāṇi varjaya  bādhakā buddhadharmāṇāṃ sadasatpakṣadṛṣṭayaḥ    tīrthadoṣairvinirmuktaṃ nairātmyavanadāhakam  jājvalatyātmavādoyaṃ yugāntāgnirivotthitaḥ    khaṇḍekṣuśarkaramadhvādidadhitilaghṛtādiṣu  svarasaṃ vidyate teṣu anāsvādyaṃ na gṛhyate    pañcadhā gṛhyamāṇaśca ātmā skandhasamucchraye  na ca paśyantyavidvāṃso vidvān dṛṣṭvā vimucyate    vidyādibhiśca dṛṣṭāntaiścittaṃ naivāvadhāryate  yatra yasmādyadarthaṃ ca samūhaṃ nāvadhāryate    vilakṣaṇā hi vai dharmāścittamekaṃ na gṛhyate  aheturapravṛttiśca tārkikāṇāṃ prasajyate    cittānupaśyī ca yogī cittaṃ citte na paśyati  paśyako dṛśyanirjāto dṛśyaṃ kiṃ hetusaṃbhavam    kātyāyanasya gotrohaṃ śuddhāvāsādviniḥsṛtaḥ  deśemi dharmaṃ sattvānāṃ nirvāṇapuragāminam    paurāṇikamidaṃ vartma ahaṃ te ca tathāgatāḥ  tribhiḥ sahasraiḥ sūtrāṇāṃ nirvāṇamatyadeśayan    kāmadhātau tathārūpye na vai buddho vibudhyate  rūpadhātvakaniṣṭheṣu vītarāgeṣu budhyate    na bandhaheturviṣayā heturviṣayabandhanam  jñānabadhyāni kleśāni asidhāravrato hyayam    asatyātmani māyādyā dharmā nāstyasti vai katham  bālānāṃ khyāti tathatā kathaṃ nāsti nirātmikā    kṛtakākṛtakatvāddhi nāsti hetuḥ pravartakaḥ  anutpannamidaṃ sarvaṃ na ca bālairvibhāvyate    kāraṇāni anutpannā kṛtakāḥ pratyayāśca te  dvāvapyetau na janakau kāraṇaiḥ kalpyate katham    prākpaścādyugapaccāpi hetuṃ varṇenti tārkikāḥ  prakāśaghaṭaśiṣyādyairbhāvānāṃ janma kathyate    nābhisaṃskārikairbuddhā lakṣaṇairlakṣaṇānvitāḥ  cakravartiguṇā hyete naite buddhaprabhāṣitāḥ    buddhānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ dṛṣṭidoṣairvivarjitam  pratyātmadṛṣṭigatikaṃ sarvadoṣavighātakam    badhirāndhakāṇamūkānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ vairavṛttinām  bālānāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa brahmacaryaṃ na vidyate    āvṛtairvyañjanairdivyairlakṣaṇaiścakravartinaḥ  vyañjitaiḥ pravrajantyeke na cānye ca pravādinaḥ    vyāsaḥ kaṇādaḥ ṛṣabhaḥ kapilaḥ śākyanāyakaḥ  nirvṛte mama paścāttu bhaviṣyantyevamādayaḥ    mayi nirvṛte varṣaśate vyāso vai bhāratastathā  pāṇḍavāḥ kauravā rāmaḥ paścānmaurī bhaviṣyati    mauryā nandāśca guptāśca tato mlecchā nṛpādhamāḥ  mlecchānte śastrasaṃkṣobhaḥ śastrānte ca kaliryugaḥ  kaliyugānte lokaiśca saddharmo hi na bhāvitaḥ    evamādyānyatītāni cakravadbhramate jagat  vahnyādityasamāyogātkāmadhāturvidīryate    punaḥ saṃsthāsyate divyaṃ tasmillokaḥ pravartsyate  cātuṃ rvarṇā nṛpendrāśca ṛṣayo dharmameva ca    vedāśca yajñaṃ dānaṃ ca dharmasthā vartsyate punaḥ  ākhyāyiketihāsādyairgadyacūrṇikavārtikaiḥ  evaṃ mayā śrutādibhyo loko vai vibhramiṣyati    suraktākoṭitaṃ kṛtvā upariṣṭādvivarṇayet  nīlakardamagomayaiḥ paṭaṃ vai saṃpracitrayet  sarvavāsairvicitrāṅgastīrthyaliṅgavivarjitaḥ    śāsanaṃ deśayedyogī buddhānāmeṣa vai dhvajaḥ  vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ peyaṃ kaṭisūtraṃ ca dhārayet  upapadyamānaṃ kālena bhaikṣyaṃ vā nīcavarjitam    divyaṃ saṃjāyate svargāddvau cānyau mānuṣodbhavau  ratnalakṣaṇasaṃpanno devajanmajageśvaraḥ    svargaṃ prabhuñjate dvīpāṃścaturo dharmaśāsanaḥ  bhuktvā tu suciraṃ dvīpāṃstṛṣṇayā vipraṇaśyati    kṛtayugaśca tretā ca dvāparaṃ kalinastathā  ahaṃ cānye kṛtayuge śākyasiṃhaḥ kalau yuge    siddhārthaḥ śākyatanayo viṣṇurvyāso maheśvaraḥ  evamādyāni tīrthyāni nirvṛte me bhaviṣyati    evaṃ mayā śrutādibhyaḥ śākyasiṃhasya deśanā  itihāsaṃ purāvṛttaṃ vyāsasyaitadbhaviṣyati    viṣṇurmaheśvaraścāpi sṛṣṭitvaṃ deśayiṣyati  evaṃ me nirvṛte paścādevamādyaṃ bhaviṣyati    mātā ca me vasumatiḥ pitā vipraḥ prajāpatiḥ  kātyāyanasagotrohaṃ nāmnā vai virajo jinaḥ    campāyāṃ haṃ samutpannaḥ pitāpi ca pitāmahaḥ  somagupteti nāmnāsau somavaṃśasamudbhavaḥ    cīrṇavrataḥ pravrajitaḥ sahasraṃ deśitaṃ nayam  vyākṛtya parinirvāsye abhiṣicya mahāmatim    matirdāsyati dharmāya dharmo dāsyati mekhale  mekhalaḥ śiṣyo daurbalyātkalpānte nāśayiṣyati    kāśyapaḥ krakucchandaśca kanakaśca vināyakaḥ  ahaṃ ca virajonye vai sarve te kṛtino jināḥ    kṛte yuge tataḥ paścānmatirnāmena nāyakaḥ  bhaviṣyati mahāvīraḥ pañcajñeyāvabodhakaḥ    na dvāpare na tretāyāṃ na paścācca kalau yuge  saṃbhavo lokanāthānāṃ saṃbudhyante kṛte yuge    ahāryā lakṣaṇāyāśca acchinnadaśakaiḥ saha  moracandrasamaiścandrairuttarīyaṃ vicitrayet    dvayaṅgulaṃ tryaṅgulaṃ vāpi candraṃ candrāntaraṃ bhavet  anyathā citryamānaṃ hi lobhanīyaṃ hi bāliśān    rāgāgniṃ śamayennityaṃ snāyādvai jñānavāriṇā  triśaraṇaṃ trisaṃdhyāsu yogī kuryātprayatnataḥ    iṣuprastarakāṣṭhādyā utkṣepādyaiḥ samīritāḥ  ekaḥ kṣiptaḥ patatyekaḥ kuśalākuśalastathā    ekaṃ ca bahudhā nāsti vailakṣaṇyānna kutracit  vāyubhā grāhakāḥ sarve kṣetravaddāyakā bhavet    yadyekaṃ bahudhā vai syātsarve hyakṛtakā bhavet  kṛtakasya vināśaḥ syāttārkikāṇāmayaṃ nayaḥ    dīpabījavadetatsyātsādṛśyādbahudhā kutaḥ  ekaṃ hi bahudhā bhavati tārkikāṇāmayaṃ nayaḥ    na tilājjāyate mudgo na vrīhiryavahetukaḥ  godhūmadhānyajātāni ekaṃ hi bahudhā katham    pāṇiniṃ śabdanetāramakṣapādo bṛhaspatiḥ  lokāyatapraṇetāro brahmā garbho bhaviṣyati    kātyāyanaḥ sūtrakartā yajñavalkastathaiva ca  bhuḍhukajyotiṣādyāni bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge    balī puṇyakṛtāllokātprajābhāgyādbhaviṣyati  rakṣakaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ rājā balī mahīpatiḥ    vālmīko masurākṣaśca kauṭilya āśvalāyanaḥ  ṛṣayaśca mahābhāgā bhaviṣyanti anāgate    siddhārthaḥ śākyatanayo bhūtāntaḥ pañcacūḍakaḥ  vāgbaliratha medhāvī paścātkāle bhaviṣyati    ajinaṃ daṇḍakāṣṭhaṃ ca mekhalācakramaṇḍalam  dadāti brahmā maheśvaro vanabhūmau vyavasthite    bhaviṣyati mahāyogī nāmnā vai virajo muniḥ  mokṣasya deśakaḥ śāstā munīnāmeṣa vai dhvajaḥ    brahmā brahmaśataiḥ sārdhaṃ devaiśca bahubhirmama  ajinaṃ prapātya gaganāttatraivāntarhito vaśī    sarvacitrāṇi vāsāṃsi bhaikṣyapātraṃ suraiḥ saha  indro virūḍhakādyāśca vanabhūmau dadanti me    anutpādavādahetviṣṭojāto jāyeta vā punaḥ  sādhayiṣyatyanutpādaṃ vāṅbhātraṃ kīrtyate tu vai    tasyāvidyā kāraṇaṃ teṣāṃ cittānāṃ saṃpravartitā  antarā kimavasthāsau yāvadrūpaṃ na jānati    samanantarapradhvastaṃ cittamanyatpravartate  rūpaṃ na tiṣṭhate kiṃcitkimālambya pravartsyate    yasmādyatra pravarteta cittaṃ vitathahetukam  na prasiddhaṃ kathaṃ tasya kṣaṇabhaṅgovadhāryate    yogināṃ hi samāpattiḥ suvarṇajinadhātavaḥ  ābhāsvaravimānāni abhedyā lokakāraṇāt    sthitayaḥ prāptidharmāśca buddhānāṃ jñānasaṃpadaḥ  bhikṣutvaṃ samayaprāptirdṛṣṭā vai kṣaṇikā katham    gandharvapuramāyādyā rūpā vai kṣaṇikā katham  abhūtikā ca bhūtāni bhūtāḥ kiṃcitkva cāgatau    avidyāhetukaṃ cittamanādimatisaṃcitam  utpādabhaṅgasaṃbaddhaṃ tārkikaiḥ saṃprakalpyate    dvividhaḥ sāṃkhyavādaśca pradhānātpariṇāmikam  pradhāne vidyate kāryaṃ kāryaṃ svātmaprasādhitam    pradhānaṃ saha bhāvena guṇabhedaḥ prakīrtitaḥ  kāryakāraṇavaicitryaṃ pariṇāme na vidyate    yathā hi pāradaḥ śuddha upakleśairna lipyate  ālayaṃ hi tathā śuddhamāśrayaḥ sarvadehinām    hiṅgugandhaḥ palāṇḍuśca garbhiṇyā garbhadarśanam  lavaṇādibhiśca lāvaṇyaṃ bījavatkiṃ na vartate    anyatve ca tadanyatve ubhayaṃ nobhaye tathā  astitvaṃ nirupādānaṃ na ca nāsti na saṃskṛtam    aśvavadvidyate hyātmā skandhairgobhāvavarjitam  saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtaṃ vācyamavaktavyaṃ svabhāvakam    yuktyāgamābhyāṃ durdṛṣṭyā tarkadṛṣṭyā malīkṛtam  anirdhāryaṃ vadantyātmā nopādāne na cānyataḥ    doṣanirdhāraṇā hyeṣāṃ skandhenātmā vibhāvyate  ekatvena tadanyatvena na ca budhyanti tārkikāḥ    darpaṇe udake netre yatha bimbaṃ pradṛśyate  ekatvānyatvarahitastathā skandheṣu pudgalaḥ    bhāvyaṃ vibhāvanādhyātā mārgaḥ satyā ca darśanam  etatrayaṃ vibhāvento mucyante hi kudarśanaiḥ    dṛṣṭaṃ naṣṭaṃ yathā vidyuccakraṃ chidragṛhe yathā  pariṇāmaḥ sarvadharmāṇāṃ bālairiva na kalpayet    bhāvābhāvena nirvāṇaṃ bālānāṃ cittamohanam  āryadarśanasadbhāvādyathāvasthānadarśanāt    utpādabhaṅgarahitaṃ bhāvābhāvavivarjitam  lakṣyalakṣaṇanirmuktaṃ pariṇāmaṃ vibhāvayet    tīrthyavādavinirmuktaṃ nāmasaṃsthānavarjitam  adhyātmadṛṣṭinilayaṃ pariṇāmaṃ vibhāvayet    saṃsparśapīḍanābhyāṃ vai devānāṃ nārakāṇi ca  antarābhavikā nāsti vijñānena pravartitā    jarajāṇḍajasaṃsvedādyā antarābhavasaṃbhavāḥ  sattvakāyā yathā citrā gatyāgatyāṃ vibhāvayet    yuktyāgamavyapetāni niḥkleśapakṣakṣayāvahā  tīrthyadṛṣṭipralāpāni matimānna samācaret    ādau nirdhāryate ātmā upādānādviśeṣayet  anirdhārya viśeṣanti vandhyāputraṃ viśiṣyate    paśyāmi sattvān divyena prajñāmāṃsavivarjitam  saṃsāraskandhanirmuktaṃ mūrtimān sarvadehinām    durvarṇasuvarṇagataṃ muktāmuktaviśeṣaṇam  divyaṃ saṃskāravigataṃ saṃskārasthaṃ prapaśyate    mūrtimān gatisaṃdhau vai tārkikāṇāmagocaram  atikrāntamānuṣyagatimahaṃ nānye kutārkikāḥ    nāstyātmā jāyate cittaṃ kasmādetatpravartate  nadīdīpabījavattasya nirgamaḥ kiṃ na kathyate    anutpanne ca vijñāne ajñānādi na vidyate  tadabhāve na vijñānaṃ saṃtatyā jāyate katham    adhvatrayamanadhvaśca avaktavyaśca pañcamaḥ  jñeyametaddhi buddhānāṃ tārkikaiḥ saṃprakīrtyate    avaktavyaśca saṃskārairjñānaṃ saṃskārahetukam  gṛhṇāti saṃskāragataṃ jñānaṃ saṃskāraśabditam    asmin satīdaṃ bhavati pratyayāścāpyahetukāḥ  vyañjakenopadiśyante tadabhāvānna kārakam    pavanaṃ hi vahnerdahanaṃ preraṇe na tu saṃbhave  prerya nirvāyate tena kathaṃ sattvaprasādhakāḥ    saṃskṛtāsaṃskṛtaṃ vācyamupādānavivarjitam  kathaṃ hi sādhakastasya vahnirbālairvikalpyate    anyonyasya balādhānādvahnirvai jāyate nṛṇām  sattvaḥ pravartitaḥ kena vahnivatkalpyate yataḥ    skandhāyatanakadambasya manādyākāraṇo nu vai  nairātmā sārthavannityaṃ cittena saha vartate    dvāvetau bhāsvarau nityaṃ kāryakāraṇavarjitau  agnirhyasādhakasteṣāṃ na ca budhyanti tārkikāḥ    cittaṃ sattvāśca nirvāṇaṃ prakṛtyā bhāsurā nu vai  doṣairanādikaiḥ kliṣṭā abhinnā gaganopamāḥ    hastiśayyādivacchāyā stīrthyadṛṣṭyā malīkṛtāḥ  manovijñānasaṃchannā agnirādyairviśodhitāḥ    dṛṣṭāśca te yathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā kleśā vidāritāḥ  dṛṣṭāntagahanaṃ hitvā gatāste āryagocaram    jñānajñeyavibhāgena anyatvaṃ kalpyate yataḥ  na ca budhyanti durmedhā avaktavyaśca kathyate    bherī yathā candanajā bālaiḥ kurvanti nānyathā  candanāgarusaṃkāśaṃ tathā jñānaṃ kutārkikaiḥ    utthitaḥ khalubhaktaśca pātrasaṃśritamātrakam  doṣairmukhavikārādyaiḥ śuddhaṃ bhaktaṃ samācaret    imaṃ nayaṃ yonuminoti yuktitaḥ prasādavān yogaparo hyakalpanaḥ  anāśrito hyarthaparo bhavedasau hiraṇmayīṃ dharmagatiṃ pradīpayet    bhāvābhāvapratyayamohakalpanā kudṛṣṭijālaṃ samalaṃ hi tasya tu  sarāgadoṣapratighaṃ nivartate nirañjano buddhakaraiśca sicyate    tīrthyā kāraṇadigmūḍhā anye pratyayavihvalāḥ  anye ahetusadbhāvāducchedaṃ āryamāsthitāḥ    vipākapariṇāmaśca vijñānasya manasya ca  mano hyālayasaṃbhūtaṃ vijñānaṃ ca manobhavam    ālayātsarvacittāni pravartanti taraṃgavat  vāsanāhetukāḥ sarve yathāpratyayasaṃbhavāḥ    kṣaṇabhedasaṃkalābaddhāḥ svacittārthavigrāhiṇaḥ  saṃsthānalakṣaṇākārā manocakṣvādisaṃbhavāḥ    anādidoṣasaṃbaddhamarthābhāvāsanoditam  bahirdhā dṛśyate cittaṃ tīrthadṛṣṭinivāraṇam    taddhetukamevānyattadālambya pravartate  yadā saṃjāyate dṛṣṭiḥ saṃsāraśca pravartate    māyāsvapnanibhā bhāvā gandharvanagaropamāḥ  marīcyudakacandrābhāḥ svavikalpaṃ vibhāvayet    vṛttibhedāttu tathatā samyagjñānaṃ tadāśrayam  māyāśūraṃgamādīni samādhīni parāṇi ca    bhūmipraveśāllabhate abhijñā vaśitāni ca  jñānamāyopamaṃ kāyamabhiṣiktaṃ ca saugatam    nivartate yadā cittaṃ nivṛttaṃ paśyato jagat  muditāṃ labhate bhūmiṃ buddhabhūmiṃ labhanti ca    āśrayeṇa nivṛttena viśvarūpo maṇiryathā  karoti sattvakṛtyāni pratibimbaṃ yathā jale    sadasatpakṣanirmuktamubhayaṃ nobhayaṃ na ca  pratyekaśrāvakīyābhyāṃ niṣkrāntā saptamī bhavet    pratyātmadṛṣṭadharmāṇāṃ bhūtabhūmiviśodhitam  bāhyatīrthyavinirmuktaṃ mahāyānaṃ vinirdiśet    parāvṛttirvikalpasya cyutināśavivarjitam  śaśaromamaṇiprakhyaṃ muktānāṃ deśayennayam    yathā hi grantho granthena yuktyā yuktistathā yadi  ato yuktirbhavedyuktimanyathā tu na kalpayet    cakṣuḥ karma ca tṛṣṇā ca avidyāyoniśastathā  cakṣūrūpe manaścāpi āvilasya manastathā    ityāryasaddharmalaṅkāvatāro nāma mahāyānasūtraṃ sagāthakaṃ samāptamiti  ye dharmā hetuprabhavā hetuṃ teṣāṃ tathāgato hyavadat  teṣāṃ ca yo nirodho evaṃ vādī mahāśramaṇaḥ
